DOROTHY E. IRMAK B.A., CERT. ED.

İngilizce Bilimsel Metinleri Anlama ve Çeviri Kılavuzu

BİLİM TEKNİK YAYINEVİ

İÇİNDEKİLER

A. There + olmak + isim (Sayfa 38)

b) Do, does, did + özne + mastar (Sayfa 52)

A. ...ing + isim (Sayfa 81)

B. İsim + ...ing + isim (Sayfa 84)

A. ...ed + isim (Sayfa 85)

B. Zarf + past participle + isim (Sayfa 88)

A. ...ing + isim (Sayfa 112)

B. Edattan sonra gelen fiil (+ nesnesi) (Sayfa 112)

XVII. ...ing + nesne... (Sayfa 113)

A. on/by/in/without + ...ing (+ nesnesi) (Sayfa 116)

B. when/while/before/after/since + ...ing (+ nesnesi) (Sayfa 118)

C. when/if/unless/although/until/as/where + past participle... (Sayfa 120)

Faydalı mutat cümle takımları (Sayfa 127)

II. BÖLÜM

I. Zarf cümleciği (Sayfa 164)

A. Zaman (Sayfa 164)

a) before (Sayfa 164)

b) after (Sayfa 169)

c) when (Sayfa 172)

d) since (Sayfa 181)

e) while/as (Sayfa 182)

f) until (Sayfa 185)

B. Sebep (Sayfa 187)

a) because (Sayfa 187)

b) since (Sayfa 191)

c) as (Sayfa 192)

C. 'Although' (Sayfa 194)

D. Derece (Sayfa 198)

E. Maksat (Sayfa 201)

F. Netice (Sayfa 204)

G. Şart (Sayfa 206)

a) if... (Sayfa 206)

b) unless (Sayfa 213)

II. Mukayese strüktürleri (Sayfa 216)

A. Basit (Sayfa 216)

B. 'than' (Sayfa 218)

C. 'as...as, the same...as' (Sayfa 222)

III. Sıfat cümleciği (Sayfa 224)

a) Who (Sayfa 224)

b) Which (Sayfa 227)

c) Where (Sayfa 231)

d) Whom (Sayfa 233)

e) Edat ile başlayan... (Sayfa 234)

f) Whose (Sayfa 236)

g) İşaret kelimesi olmayan... (Sayfa 239)

IV. İsim cümleciği (Sayfa 240)

a) Soru kelimesi (Sayfa 241)

b) "that" (Sayfa 244)

c) "if/whether" (Sayfa 247)

d) "the fact that" (Sayfa 248)

V. It + to be + sıfat/past part. + that... (Sayfa 251)

VI. It + to be + sıfat/past part. + mastar + that... (Sayfa 254)

VII. Neden ve etki strüktürleri (Sayfa 256)

Cetvel I (Sayfa 260)

Cetvel II (Sayfa 261)

Sınıflandırılmış metinler (Sayfa 262)

Adverbial clauses only (Sayfa 262)

Adjectival clauses only (Sayfa 268)

Adjectival and Adverbial clauses (Sayfa 273)

Noun clauses only (Sayfa 287)

İngilizce bir metni anlamak veya Türkçeye çevirmek için önemli cümle yapılarının özelliklerini tanımak lazımdır. Bu kitap, kolayından başlayarak en önemli cümle yapılarını tanımak ve tercüme etmek için öğrenciye gerekli alıştırmaları sağlar.

I. A Özne + olmak fiili + İsim

1. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The student is a doctor.

The man is a professor.

The woman is a lawyer.

The book is a dictionary.

The building is a hospital.

The statement is a confession.

The paper is a guarantee.

The experiment is a test.

The chapter is a summary.

The lesson is a preparation.

The lesson is an experiment.

The method is an experiment.

The author is a woman.

The economist is an expert.

The punishment is a fine.

The signature is a forgery.

Sözlük

author: yazar

building: bina

chapter: bölüm (kitap)

confession: itiraf

economist: iktisatçı, ekonomist

experiment: deney

expert: uzman

fine: para cezası

forgery: taklit, sahte

guarantee: garanti

hospital: hastane

lawyer: hukukçu, avukat

preparation: hazırlık

punishment: ceza

signature: imza

statement: beyanat, demeç

summary: özet

Anlama soruları

What is the student?

What is the man?

What is the woman?

What is the book?

What is the building?

What is the statement?

What is the paper?

What is the experiment?

What is the chapter?

What is the lesson?

What is the lesson?

What is the economist?

What is the author?

What is the economist?

What is the punishment?

What is the signature?

Alıştırmalar

2. Yukarıda yazılan 1-16 sayılı cümleleri olumsuz şekle koyunuz ve Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: The student is not a doctor. Öğrenci doktor değildir.

3. Yukarıda yazılan 1-16 sayılı cümleleri geçmiş zamana koyunuz ve Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: The student was a doctor. Öğrenci doktordu.

4. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Light is energy.

Heat is energy.

Currency is money.

Capital is an investment.

Starch is a carbohydrate.

Meat is a protein.

A contract is an agreement.

Heredity is a factor.

Iron is a metal.

Gold is a metal.

Oxygen is an element.

Oil is a mineral.

Bacteria are organisms.

Lime is an alkali.

Sözlük

agreement: anlaşma

capital: sermaye

contract: akit, sözleşme

currency: rayiç, geçerli para

gold: altın

heat: ısı

heredity: irsiyet, kalıtım

investment: yatırım

iron: demir

light: ışık

lime: kireç

metal: maden, metal

oil: petrol, yağ

starch: nişasta

Anlama soruları

What is light?

What is heat?

What is currency?

What is capital?

What is starch?

What is meat?

What is a contract?

What is heredity?

What is iron?

What is gold?

What is oxygen?

What is oil?

What are bacteria?

What is lime?

Alıştırma

5. Yukarıda yazılan 1-14 sayılı cümleleri soru şekline koyunuz ve Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: Is light energy? Işık enerji midir?

B Özne + olmak fiili + sıfat

6. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The ground is wet.

The cost is high.

The price is low.

The answer is wrong.

The explanation is long.

The machine is expensive.

The results are important.

The expenses are high.

The experiments are important.

The substances are pure.

The substance is impure.

The results are favourable.

The costs are low.

The reactions are slow.

Bacteria are present.

Profits are high.

cost: maliyet, fiyat

expenses: masraf, harcama

expensive: pahalı

experiment: deney

explanation: açıklama

favourable: uygun, olumlu

ground: yer, zemin

important: önemli

impure: saf olmayan, karışık

present: mevcut, var

price: fiyat

profit: kâr, kazanç

pure: saf, temiz

reaction: reaksiyon, tepki

result: sonuç

substance: madde

wet: ıslak, nemli

wrong: yanlış

Anlama soruları

What is wet?

What is high?

What is low?

What is wrong?

What is long?

What is expensive?

What are pure?

What are favourable?

What are low?

Alıştırma

7. Yukarıda yazılı 1-16 sayılı cümleleri olumsuz şekle koyunuz ve Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: The ground is not wet. Yer ıslak değildir.

8. Yukarıda yazılan 1-16 sayılı cümlelerin fiillerini MAY BE şeklini kullanarak 'OLABİLİR' diye Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: The ground may be wet. Yer ıslak olabilir.

9. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The atmosphere is dense.

The argument is illogical.

The belief is mistaken.

The circumstances are difficult.

The result is doubtful.

Heredity is important.

The accident was serious.

The results are important.

The increase was gradual.

The improvement was gradual.

The punishment is serious.

The author is famous.

The argument is logical.

The experiment is successful.

Phosphorus is poisonous.

The method is successful.

argument: tez, sav, tartışma

atmosphere: atmosfer

gradual: tedrici, kademe kademe

increase: artma, artım

logical: mantıklı, mantıki

method: metot, yöntem

mistaken: yanlış, hatalı

phosphorus: fosfor

poisonous: zehirli

serious: ciddi, ağır

successful: başarılı

What is serious?

Örnek: The atmosphere may not be dense. Atmosfer yoğun olmayabilir.

C Özne + olmak fiili + Sıfat + İsim

Phosphorus is a poisonous element.

Water is a colourless liquid.

Tungsten is a rare element.

D Özne + olmak fiili + edat takımı

16. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The student is in the train.

The explanation is at the end.

The building is on the other side.

The test-tube is on my table.

The summary is at the end.

The papers are on my table.

The buildings are in the centre.

The chapters are at the end.

The workers are in the factory.

The factories are outside the town.

The substances are in the liquid.

The liquids are in the test-tubes.

The reports are from the employers.

The answers are on this paper.

The statements are in this report.

The bacteria are in the tissues.

Lime is in the soil.

17. Yukarıda yazılan cümleleri (1-22) gelecek zamana koyunuz ve Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: The student will be in the train. Öğrenci trende olacaktır.

18. Yukarıda yazılan cümleleri (1-22) geçmiş zamana çeviriniz:

Örnek: The student was in the train. Öğrenci trende idi.

19. Yukarıda yazılan cümleleri geçmiş zamana, olumsuz şekle çeviriniz:

Örnek: The student was not in the train. Öğrenci trende değildi.

II. A İsim + edat takımı

Edat takımı, önünde gelen ismi tamamlıyor. Tercüme edilirken bazen 'ki', 'olan' veya 'bulunan' ilave edilir.

Örnek: the house on the corner  köşedeki ev / köşede olan ev / köşede bulunan ev

20. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

the workers in the factory

the statement in the newspaper

the papers on my table

the photograph in the newspaper

the difference between the results

the molecules in the liquid

the molecules in the gas

the policy of the government

government by the people

the examination of the doctor

damage to the head

the ideas in this chapter

the bones in the arm

the heat in the metal

the cure for this disease

injection under the skin

preparation for an examination

employment in the factories

a substance in the blood

the distance from this point

the water under the ground

the situation in America

Sözlük

bone: kemik

chapter: bölüm

cure: tedavi

damage: zarar, incinme

difference: fark

disease: hastalık

distance: mesafe, uzaklık

employment: çalışma, iş

factory: fabrika

government: hükümet

ground: yer, zemin

heat: ısı

idea: fikir

injection: enjeksiyon

liquid: sıvı

molecule: molekül

point: nokta

policy: tutum, politika

preparation: hazırlık

result: netice, sonuç

situation: durum

skin: deri

statement: ifade, beyan, demeç

substance: madde

21. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The employer of these men is at the office.

The explanation of this problem is at the end.

The machine for cutting paper is in the factory.

The substance in the test-tube is from this bottle.

The answer to this problem is in the book.

The market for these goods is in the Far East.

The building in the centre of the town is between the railway and the river.

The book about Turkey is on the table.

The summary of the chapter is at the end.

The papers for the examination are on my table.

The buildings on the corner are in the centre of the city.

The chapters on Turkey are at the end.

The factories inside the town are near the river.

The substances in the liquid are from this bottle.

The liquids in the test-tubes are in the laboratory.

The answers to the questions are on this paper.

The statements of the workers are in this report.

The coal in this area is near the surface.

The translation of these sentences is on the next page.

Nutrients in the soil are near the surface.

Sözlük

building: bina

centre: orta, merkez

chapter: bölüm

coal: kömür

corner: köşe

employer: işveren

explanation: açıklama

factory: fabrika

goods: eşya, mal

laboratory: laboratuvar

liquid: sıvı

machine: makine

market: pazar, piyasa

nutrient: besin maddesi

railway: demir yolu

report: rapor

substance: madde

summary: özet

surface: yüzey

test-tube: deney tüpü

translation: tercüme, çeviri

Alıştırmalar

22. Yukarıda yazılan 1-20 sayılı cümlelerin fiillerini 'SHOULD BE' şeklini kullanarak 'OLMALIDIR' diye Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: The employer of these men should be at the office. Bu adamların işvereni büroda olmalıdır.

23. 1-22 sayılı aşağıda verilmiş cümlelerde bulunan edat takımlarını parantez içine alıp niteledikleri isimlere bağlayarak tercüme ediniz:

The activities of the research workers are in this report.

The results of their investigations are in the report.

The results of these experiments will be in this report.

The decision of the committee was in favour of their activities.

The majority of the workers were in favour of the decisions.

The details of the experiment are in this report.

The answers to all these questions are at the end of the book.

The object of the research project will be at the beginning of the report.

The details of the study were not in the report.

The comprehension questions for these sentences are at the end of the exercise.

The bacteria of this disease are in the tissues of the lung.

The date of the next meeting is on the notice board.

The report of the last meeting may be on the notice board.

The equipment for the next experiment is not in the laboratory.

The statement from the manager was in today's newspaper.

The materials for the next experiment are in this box.

The reasons for their refusal are in this statement.

The list of names of patients from that hospital is in the records.

The records of all the students are in these files.

The address of every hospital in London is in our records.

The names and addresses of all our patients are in these files.

The oil in this area is below the level of the sea.

Sözlük

activity: faaliyet, eylem

committee: heyet, komisyon

comprehension: anlama

date: tarih

decision: karar

detail: detay, ayrıntı

disease: hastalık

equipment: alet, cihaz

experiment: tecrübe, deney

file: dosya

hospital: hastane

in favour of: lehinde, destekliyor

investigation: inceleme, tahkikat

level: seviye

lung: akciğer

manager: müdür

majority: çoğunluk

material: malzeme

meeting: toplantı

notice board: ilan tahtası

object: gaye, amaç, nesne

oil: petrol, yağ

patient: hasta

project: proje

reason: neden, sebep

record: kayıt, dosya

refusal: reddetme

report: rapor

research: araştırma

result: sonuç

statement: beyan, demeç

study: etüt, inceleme

tissue: doku

Anlama soruları

What are in this report? Where are the activities of the research workers?

What are in the report? Where are the results of their investigations?

What will be in this report? Where are the results of these experiments?

What was in favour of their activities?

What were in favour of the decisions?

What are in this report? Where are the details of the experiment?

What are at the end of the book? Where are the answers to all these questions?

What will be at the beginning of the report? Where will the object of the research project be?

What were not in the report?

What are at the end of this exercise? Where are the comprehension questions for these sentences?

What are in the tissues of the lung? Where are the bacteria of this disease?

What is on the notice board? Where is the date of the next meeting?

What may be on the notice board? Where may the report of the last meeting be?

What is not in the laboratory?

What was in today's newspaper? Where was the statement from the manager?

What are in these files? Where are the names and addresses of all our patients?

What is below the level of the sea? Where is the oil in this area?

C. Zamir + 'of the' + isim

Zamirlerin en mühimleri:

some: bazı, bir kısmı

most: çoğu

another: başka bir

all: hepsi

each: her biri

part: bir kısım

several: birkaç

a little: az, bir miktar

half: yarısı

none: hiçbirbiri

a number of: birkaç

one, two, three (v.s.): bir, iki, üç...

Yukarıdaki zamirler, 'OF THE + İSİM'den önce gelirse, aşağıda gösterilen şekilde Türkçeye çevrilir:

two of the books: kitapların ikisi

another of the books: kitapların bir başkası

several of the books: birkaç kitap, kitapların birkaçı

half of the books: kitapların yarısı

a number of the books: birkaç kitap

a little of the bread: ekmeğin az bir miktarı

The production of raw materials has increased recently.

The produce of Turkey has found a market in many parts of the world.

They have not yet discovered the existence of coal in that area.

III. A. Fiil + Edat takımı

Bu strüktürde, edat takımı, zarf gibi ya fiili ya da bütün cümleyi tamamlar. Tercümede, fiilin yanına veya cümlenin başına yerleştirmek doğru olur.

Örnek: The student is working in the library.  Talebe kütüphanede çalışıyor.

Örnek: The student works in the library on Fridays.  Cuma günleri talebe kütüphanede çalışır.

Alıştırma:

34. 1-14

a) Siyah yazılı olan fiili, öznesiyle beraber tercüme ediniz.

b) Parantez içinde bulunan edat takımını Türkçeye çeviriniz.

c) Edat takımını fiile yakın veya cümle başında yerleştirerek bütün cümleyi tercüme ediniz.

We describe this method (in the next chapter).

We find the measurements (on this page).

We employ this method (for this experiment).

We cured that disease (in two months).

We injected the substance (into the muscle).

We used the wood (for building).

We pumped the water (to the surface).

We injected the substance (under the skin).

We prepared the students (for the examination).

We measured the volume (before heating it).

We use coal (for this purpose).

We employ these workers (for the building).

We divided the work (according to this principle).

Man invented fire (thousands of years ago).

Anlama soruları

Where do we describe this method?

Where do we find the measurements?

Where do we employ this method?

When did we cure that disease?

Where did we inject the substance?

Where did we use the wood?

Where did we pump the water?

Where did we inject the substance?

For what did we prepare the students?

When did we measure the volume?

For what did we use the coal?

For what did we employ the workers?

According to what did we divide the work?

When did man invent fire?

B Edat takımı + edat takımı

Örnek: after the invention of fire  Ateşin icadından sonra

Arka arkaya gelen iki (veya daha fazla) edat takımı birbirini tamamlarsa, sonundan başlayarak başına doğru tercüme edilir.

36. Yukarıda bulunan 1-26 cümle parçaları aşağıda birer cümle içinde kullanılmıştır. Bu cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Transport was very difficult before the invention of the wheel.

In this form of government parliament is responsible to the people.

The first bacillus came to light during a study of this disease.

The invention of writing was an important event in the history of civilisation.

War has always existed during the long history of man.

Workers receive payment according to the division of labour.

These statistics predict the ages according to the expectancy of life.

He cannot decide the case without proof of guilt.

Most of the wealth of the country comes from the production of raw materials.

He measured the calcium content in the blood of the animal.

Lactic acid accumulates in the muscles of the leg.

These mistakes are the cause of the difference in the results.

The emission of light comes from the vibration of the molecules.

The government requires these raw materials for the duration of the war.

They could not decide on a course of action because of the difficulty of the problem.

Many new developments took place after the discovery of the element.

Rebuilding will cost thousands of pounds according to their estimation of the damage.

37. Aşağıda verilen cümlelerde bulunan edat takımlarını parantez içine alıp yerli yerine koyarak bütün cümleyi tercüme ediniz:

The transport of heavy objects became easier after the invention of the wheel.

The responsibility of government falls upon parliament in this form of government.

During a study of the disease of leprosy the bacillus of this disease came to light.

The long history of man is full of accounts of war, poverty and disease.

After the discovery of the use of electricity for lighting purposes, the lighting of large cities became easy and efficient.

One of the most important events in the long history of man is the invention of writing several thousands of years ago.

The division of labour is one of the most important features in the development of the life of a community.

The increase in the expectancy of life is one of the chief indications of a rising standard of living in any community.

The burden of proof of guilt does not fall on the accused.

After the discovery of radium, protection from the effects of radiation became a matter of importance in science.

The existence of coal was one of the important reasons for intense industrialisation in England during the 19th century.

The increase in the production of raw materials has caused an increase in the wealth of the country as a whole.

The agricultural areas of Turkey supply most of the produce both for export and for home consumption.

Nationalisation of the coal industry is essential in view of the increase in the consumption of coal in the country.

Radiation from space causes the necessity for protective measures to prevent damage to equipment.

An article in the newspaper describes the dangers of the situation.

Loss of heat into the surrounding air causes condensation on the surface of the solid.

The vibration of the molecules in thin gases causes an emission of light in the tubes.

The calcium content in the blood of the animal increased.

The accumulation of lactic acid in the muscles of the leg causes tiredness.

The difference in the results of these experiments is due to the mistakes in measuring.

The raw materials from the mines in this area are of high quality.

The decision on a course of action caused many difficulties.

The discovery of the element led to many new developments in this field.

The government will supply the money to cover the cost of rebuilding.

IV. Özne + Geçişli fiil + nesne

Nesne, fiilden HEMEN sonra gelen isimdir. Cümleyi anlamak için nesneyi (varsa) bulup, fiilden evvel tercüme etmek lazımdır.

Örnek:

Özne + Fiil + Nesne  The man painted the house.

Özne + Nesne + Fiil  Adam evi boyadı.

Alıştırma:

40. 1-20

a) Siyah yazılı fiili, öznesiyle beraber tercüme ediniz.

b) Siyah yazılı fiilden hemen sonra gelen ismi bulup tercüme ediniz.

c) Fiilden önce yerleştirip bütün cümleyi tercüme ediniz.

Örnek: 1) The professor explained the problem.

a) Profesör izah etti.

b) Problem, problemi.

c) Profesör problemi izah etti.

The students performed the experiment.

The specialist cured the disease.

The scientist injected the substance.

The workers used the raw materials.

The student measured the volume.

The workers divided the work.

The doctors treated the disease.

The plant absorbed the water.

Edison invented the electric bulb.

Sayfa 38

V. There + to be + İsim

Buna kısaca (Var/Yok strüktürü) denir. There + olmak fiilinden sonra gelen ismi bulup özne olarak kabul etmek gerekir. Tercüme şu şekilde yapılır:

There is a house. Bir ev vardır.

There wasn't time. / There was no time. Vakit yoktu.

There is an examination. Bir imtihan vardır.

Alıştırma 44: 1-22 Türkçeye çeviriniz.

There is an examination.

There is a test.

There is a possibility.

There is a tendency.

There is a translation.

There is a form.

There is a hope.

There is an improvement.

There is a theory.

There is a supply.

There is a wire.

There is a vibration.

There is a temperature.

There is a type.

There is a statement.

There is a suggestion.

There is a summary.

There is a source.

There is a solution.

There is a similarity.

There is a profit.

There is a condition.

Sözlük

condition: şart, koşul

examination: imtihan, sınav

improvement: iyileşme, gelişme

profit: kâr

similarity: benzerlik

solution: çare, çözüm

source: kaynak, menba

statement: beyan, demeç

suggestion: teklif, öneri

summary: özet

supply: stok, miktar, arz

temperature: sıcaklık

tendency: meyil, eğilim

test: deney, test

theory: teori

translation: tercüme, çeviri

type: tip, stil, örnek

vibration: vibrasyon, titreşim

wire: tel

Anlama soruları: 1-22 What is there?

Alıştırma 45: 1-22 Geçmiş zamana çevirip tercüme ediniz. (Örnek: There was an examination. Bir imtihan vardı.)

Aynı cümleler olumsuz şekilde aşağıda verilmiştir. 'A, AN' yerine 'NO' konmuştur.

Alıştırma 48: Yukarıda 1-22 sayılı cümlelerdeki IS NO yerine ISN'T ANY kullanarak okuyunuz. Anlamında hiçbir fark yoktur. (Örnek: There isn't any examination. İmtihan yoktur.)

B. 1-22 Numaralı cümlelerdeki isimden önce birer sıfat ilave edilmiştir.

Sayfa 40

Bu (Var/Yok strüktürü) olmak fiilinin diğer zamanları ve şekilleri ile bulunabilir. Şöyle:

Olumlu

Anlamı

Olumsuz

Anlamı

there will be

olacak

won't be / will not be / will be no

there may / might be

olabilir

may not be / be no

there can / could be

olabilir / olabilirdi

cannot be / could not be

there has / have been

olmuştur

has / have not been

there must / should be

olmalıdır

must not be / should not be

there must / should have been

olmalıydı

must / should not have been

Alıştırma 51: Aşağıda verilmiş olan cümleleri, yukarıda verilmiş tercümelere göre Türkçeye çeviriniz.

(Örnek: There will be no long examination. Uzun bir imtihan olmayacaktır.)

There will be a long examination.

There will be a short test.

There may be a faint possibility.

There may be a slight tendency.

There may be a good translation.

There may be no new form.

There might be a faint hope.

There have been no great improvements.

There have been many new theories.

There may be large supplies.

There must be a thin wire.

There may be a slight vibration.

There could be a high temperature.

There have been several new types.

Sayfa 41

There must be no false statement.

There may be many useful suggestions.

There must be a short summary.

There will be a new source.

There might be a hopeful solution.

There could be a slight similarity.

There will be no large profit.

There will be an important condition.

Alıştırma 52: Aşağıda yazılı 23-42 sayılı cümlelerin edat takımlarını yerlerine koyup Türkçeye tercüme ediniz.

(Örnek: There will be a long examination in English next week. Gelecek hafta İngilizcede uzun bir imtihan olacaktır.) 23. There will be no long examination in English next week. 24. There will be a short test in Geology this afternoon. 25. There may be a faint possibility of improvement next year. 26. There may be a slight tendency towards improvement soon. 27. There will be a good translation of this work in the library. 28. There may be a new form of power within the next few years. 29. There could be a faint hope of improvement soon. 30. There have been no great improvements in this field recently. 31. There have been many new theories during the last few years. 32. There may be large supplies of this raw material in Asia. 33. There must be a thin wire from the electrode to the battery. 34. There could be a high temperature at a later stage of the disease. 35. There may be a slight vibration from the machinery. 36. There have been several new types of equipment recently. 37. There must be no false statement in this report. 38. There may be many useful suggestions from the committee. 39. There must be a short summary at the end of the chapter. 40. There will be a new source of raw material in the next 10 years. 41. There might be a hopeful solution to the question soon. 42. There could be a slight similarity between the different types of plant.

Sözlük

area: saha, alan

battery: pil, akümülatör

different: farklı

power: kudret, güç

raw material: ham madde

report: rapor

soon: yakın zamanda

stage: devre, aşama

towards: ...ye doğru

within: zarfında, içinde

Sayfa 42

Sayfa 49

VI. Soru Strüktürleri

a) Soru kelimesi + fiil + özne.

(Örnek: Where are you? Cümle soru kelimesiyle başlar, çekimli fiil ve öznesi yer değiştirir.)

b) Soru kelimesi + do, does, did + özne + mastar

Cümle soru kelimesiyle başlar, çekimli fiil 'do, does' veya 'did' ile mastar kullanılır. (Örnek: Where did you go?)

Alıştırmalar

63. Aşağıda verilmiş olan soru kelimelerinin manalarını öğreniniz:

when: ne zaman

why: niye, neden

how: nasıl

what: ne

what for: ne için

whose: kimin

where: nerede, nereye

how many: kaç (tane)

how long: kaç zaman, ne kadar süre

how much: ne kadar

how far: ne kadar uzak

which: hangi(si)

who: kim

When can light travel through space?

How much is the profit this year?

When is operation necessary?

Who was the first chemist?

Who has removed the keys from the desk?

Who will profit from this development?

b) Alıştırma

65. Fiilin soru strüktürü, zamana göre 'do, does' veya 'did' + mastar şeklinde olur.

Şimdiki zaman: He laughs  Does he laugh? (Güler mi?)

Geçmiş zaman: He laughed  Did he laugh? (Güldü mü?)

B. Soru strüktürü

a) Fiil + Özne

(Örnek: Is the man here? Adam burada mıdır?)

Bu strüktürde soru kelimesi yoktur. Soru doğrudan doğruya fiil ile başlar. Tercüme ederken 'mi' takısı kullanılır.

Alıştırma 67: Cümleleri 'mi' takısı kullanarak Türkçeye çeviriniz:

(Örnek: Can the liquid absorb the gas? Sıvı gazı absorbe edebilir mi?)

Can the liquid absorb the gas?

Can the liquid dissolve the substance?

Can the reaction take place in the test tube?

Will the reaction be slow or fast?

Is the amount great or small?

Is the average high or low?

Is the community large or small?

Will there be another examination?

Will there be another war?

Has the strike begun?

Was the operation necessary?

Is the population increasing?

Has the situation changed?

Have there been any improvements?

Was there any reason for the change?

Will there be another strike next month?

Sayfa 52

b) do, does, did fiili + özne + mastar

(Örnek: Does he live here? Burada mı oturuyor? / Did the man take the keys? Adam anahtarları aldı mı?)

(Örnek: Did the liquid absorb the gas? Sıvı gazı absorbe etti mi?)

Did the liquid absorb the gas?

C. Soru strüktürü: Edat + soru kelimesi + fiil + özne

(Örnek: With whom did he live last year? Geçen sene kiminle oturuyordu?)

Bu strüktürde soru, bir edat ile başlar. Bu edat, sorudaki fiile bağlıdır.

Alıştırma 69: Aşağıda yazılı olan cümleleri tercüme ediniz.

(Örnek: For what purpose is the machine? Makine hangi maksat içindir?)

Sayfa 55

VIII. Edilgen Strüktürü (Pasif Strüktürü)

Bu strüktürde fiil hususi bir şekil alır. Zamanı 'to be' fiili kullanılarak, ana mana ise 'past participle' (yani fiilin üçüncü şekli) kullanılarak ifade edilir. Şöyle:

Şimdiki zaman: is done  yapılır

Geçmiş zaman: was/were done  yapıldı

Gelecek zaman: will be done  yapılacak

Present perfect: has/have been done  yapılmıştır

Alıştırmalar

71. Yukarıda verilmiş açıklamaya göre aşağıda verilmiş olan fiilleri uygun bir şekilde tercüme ediniz: (Örnek: has been absorbed  absorbe edilmiştir.)

has been absorbed

is obtained

has been abolished

was accepted

have been achieved

has been adjusted

was added

was adopted

have been changed

was estimated

was applied

were approved

was measured

was discovered

were classified

was made of

was composed of

is developed

will be developed

was prevented

will be prevented

has been accepted

will be obtained

was abolished

will be accepted

will be applied

has been approved

are classified

is said

were composed of

has been applied

was heated

was proved

Sözlük

to absorb: absorbe etmek

to abolish: yok etmek, kaldırmak

to accept: kabul etmek

to achieve: başarmak

to add: ilave etmek

to adjust: ayarlamak

to adopt: benimsemek, kabul etmek

to apply: uygulamak

to approve: onaylamak

to classify: sınıflandırmak

to be composed of: ...den meydana gelmek

to develop: gelişmek, geliştirmek

to discover: keşfetmek, bulmak

to estimate: tahmin etmek

to heat: ısıtmak

to measure: ölçmek

to obtain: elde etmek

to prevent: önlemek

to prove: ispat etmek

72. Yukarıda verilen 1-33 sayılı fiillere, ilk kelimesinden sonra birer 'not' ilave edilirse edilgenin olumsuz şekli meydana gelmiş olur. Fiilleri olumsuz şekilde okuyup tercüme ediniz. (Örnek: has not been absorbed  absorbe edilmemiştir.)

Sayfa 56

Alıştırma 73: Verilen örneğe göre cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

(Örnek: The gas has been absorbed by the liquid. Gaz, sıvı tarafından absorbe edilmiştir.)

The gas has been absorbed by the liquid.

Coal is obtained from the mines in northern England.

The law has been abolished recently.

The suggestion was accepted immediately.

Good results have been achieved in this field.

The machine has been adjusted.

The substance was added to the liquid.

The plan was adopted at the meeting.

The plans have been changed.

The amount was estimated at 2.5 grams.

This new method was applied in the experiment.

The new methods were approved by the scientists.

The amount of liquid was measured before the experiment.

An ancient civilisation was discovered in the Indus valley.

The discoveries were classified in three categories.

The results of all the experiments were classified.

The mixture was composed of cement, sand and water.

A new development has been achieved in this field.

Community life among primitive people has been developed.

War was prevented between the two nations.

Anlama soruları

What has been absorbed? What has absorbed the gas?

What is obtained? Where is the coal obtained?

What has been abolished? When was the law abolished?

Sayfa 57

What was accepted? When was the suggestion accepted?

What has been achieved? Where have the good results been achieved?

What has been adjusted? What has been done with the machine?

What was added to the liquid? Where was the substance added?

What was adopted at the meeting? Where was the plan adopted?

What have been changed? What has been done with the plans?

What was estimated? How much was the amount estimated at?

What was applied? Where was the new method applied?

What was approved by the scientists? What did the scientists do?

What was measured? When was the amount measured?

What was discovered? Where was the ancient civilisation discovered?

What were classified? How were the discoveries classified?

What were classified? What was done with the results?

What was the mixture composed of?

What has developed among primitive people? Where has community life developed?

What has been achieved? Where has the new development been achieved?

What was prevented? What was done?

Olumsuz Edilgen

Yukarıda yazılmış olan 'to be' fiillerine birer 'not' kelimesi katılırsa olumsuz şekil meydana gelir:

Şimdiki zaman: is not done  yapılmaz

Geçmiş zaman: was/were not done  yapılmadı

Gelecek zaman: will not be done  yapılmayacak

Present perfect: has/have not been done  yapılmamıştır

Alıştırma 74: Aşağıda verilmiş edilgen, olumsuz fiilleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

has not been performed

will not be decided

are not grown

have not been obtained

has not been damaged

will not be removed

is not solved

are not protected

is not proved

The new methods have not yet been approved.

The ancient civilisation was not discovered until recently.

B. 'By' ile tamamlanan edilgen

Bazı edilgen cümlelerde, yüklemin işi kimin veya neyin tarafından yapıldığı gösterilir. O zaman İngilizcede 'by' kelimesiyle başlayan bir edat takımı ilave edilir.

Sayfa 61

(Örnek: The book was written. Kitap yazıldı. / The book was written by a journalist. Kitap bir gazeteci tarafından yazıldı.)

Yani, yüklemdeki yazı işini bir gazetecinin yapmış olduğu belli oldu.

Alıştırma 77: Cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

(Örnek: The plan was approved by the committee. Plan heyet tarafından tasdik edildi.)

The plan was approved by the committee.

The wood was used by the builders.

The war was won by the Romans.

The law was reformed by the king.

Permission was refused by Parliament.

The new government was recognised by the United Nations.

Iron is not exported by this country.

The building was destroyed by fire.

A new government was established by the Bolshevics.

The reform was followed by improvements in administration.

The situation was improved by the new reforms.

New industrial developments were introduced by the manager.

New machines are required by the industrialists.

The factories were inspected by the new minister.

This method was introduced by Lavoisier.

This effect was observed by Newton.

The results of the experiments are affected by these changes.

The damage was done by fire and flood.

The effects were observed by the research workers.

Conditions were improved by the new reforms.

Anlama soruları

What did the committee do? Who approved the plans?

What did the builders do? Who used the wood?

What did the Romans do? Who won the war?

What did the king do? Who reformed the law?

What did Parliament do? Who refused permission?

What did the United Nations do? Who recognised the new government?

What does this country not do? Who does not export iron?

What did fire do? What destroyed the building?

What did the Bolshevics do? Who established a new government?

What did improvements in administration do? What followed reform?

What did the new reforms do? What improved the situation?

What did the manager do? Who introduced new industrial developments?

What do the industrialists do? Who require the new machines?

What did the new minister do? Who inspected the factories?

What did Lavoisier do? Who introduced this method?

What did Newton do? Who observed this effect?

What do these changes do? What affect the results of the experiments?

What did fire and flood do? What did the damage?

What did the research workers do? Who observed the effects?

What did the new reforms do? What improved conditions?

Alıştırmalar

78. Yukarıda bulunan edilgen cümlelerin fiillerine birer 'not' kelimesini katarak olumsuz şekline çeviriniz (7. cümle hariç). Cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz. (Örnek: The plan was not approved by the committee. Plan, heyet tarafından tasdik edilmedi.)

79. Bu cümleleri gelecek zamana koyunuz ve Türkçeye çeviriniz. (Örnek: The plan will be approved by the committee. Plan, heyet tarafından tasdik edilecektir.)

82. Yukarıda yazılı cümlelerin fiillerine birer 'not' kelimesini ilave ederek cümleleri olumsuz yapınız ve Türkçeye çeviriniz. (Örnek: Water cannot be absorbed. Su absorbe edilemez.)

Edilgen Fiilin Arasına Gelen Zarf

(Örnek: The book will soon be published. Kitap yakında neşredilecek.)

Örnekte görüldüğü gibi 'will be published' fiilinin arasına 'soon' zarfı konmuştur. Her türlü zarf ve zarf takımı bu şekilde fiile karışabilir. Tercüme ederken, zarfı çıkarıp fiile yakın bir yere veya cümle başına yerleştirmek doğru olur.

Alıştırma 83: Cümlelerde bulunan fiillerin arasına girmiş zarfları belirleyip, cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

(Örnek: The aims of the government will (soon) be accomplished. Hükümetin gayeleri yakında gerçekleştirilecektir.)

The aims of the government will soon be accomplished.

The arrangement of the exhibition has not yet been decided.

The attempts of the government to accomplish their policy will immediately be confirmed.

The wires from the battery to the apparatus have not yet been connected.

The cost of the government's contribution has not yet been calculated.

The decrease in the incidence of this disease will eventually be determined.

The disadvantages of the situation have not yet been discussed.

Increase in production from these districts must eventually be achieved.

The distribution of forests in Turkey was first shown on a map.

The difference between the results cannot yet be distinguished.

The distinction between the two types will doubtless be discussed.

The education of children between 5 and 15 years of age was previously neglected.

The frontiers between the two nations have frequently been disputed.

The fundamental responsibilities of the state must always be carried out.

This species was first identified by a British naturalist.

These species are never included in that category.

These effects were first observed by Robert Brown.

Excavations have recently been limited to these areas.

These objects were recently excavated from the foundations.

The function of government is therefore usually carried out by parliament.

Anlama soruları

What will soon be accomplished? When will it be accomplished?

What has not yet been decided?

What have not yet been connected?

What has not yet been calculated?

What will be determined? When will it be determined?

What are not yet apparent?

What must be achieved? When must it be achieved?

What was shown on a map? When was it shown?

What cannot yet be distinguished?

What will doubtless be discussed?

What was neglected? When was it neglected?

What have been disputed? When have they been disputed?

What must be carried out? When must they be carried out?

IX. İsim Tamlaması (Noun Completion)

Bazen bir isim diğer bir ismi niteler. Yani ilk gelen isim, takip eden ismi bir sıfatın yaptığı gibi niteler.

Sayfa 73

Örnekler

Sıfat + İsim: a high wall (yüksek bir duvar), a long lesson (uzun bir ders)

İsim + İsim: a stone wall (bir taş duvar), a history lesson (tarih dersi)

Örnekte görüldüğü gibi 'high' sıfatı nasıl 'wall' ismini nitelerse, 'stone' ismi de aynı şekilde 'wall' kelimesini niteler.

Alıştırma 86: Aşağıda verilen isim tamlamalarını Türkçeye çeviriniz:

a rubber ball

a geography lesson

gold rings

a wall map

a leather bag

the river banks

the sea shore

coast road

the stone age

iron bridge

a sugar factory

university buildings

wine glasses

life story

state control

government policy

rescue team

glass tube

farm land

cell wall

state monopoly

Sözlük

age: çağ, yaş

bank: kenar, kıyı

building: bina

cell: hücre

coast: sahil, kıyı

farm: ziraat, tarım

glass: cam, kadeh

gold: altın

government: hükümet

iron: demir

land: arazi, toprak

leather: deri

map: harita

policy: politika, siyaset

rescue: kurtarma

shore: sahil

state: devlet

team: ekip, takım

wine: şarap

A new sugar factory will be built here next year.

They are not allowed inside the university buildings.

B. Sıfat + İsim + İsim

SAYFA 81

X. Present Participle Sıfatı

A. Açıklama

-ing + isim

Fiilin "-ing" şekli, sıfat gibi kullanılır; yani isimden önce gelip o ismi niteler. Türkçede üç tercüme şekli vardır:

Örnek:

running water (karakteristiği bu, her zaman akar)  akar su

crying baby (şimdiki halde ağlıyor)  ağlayan bebek

protecting wall (korumak maksadı ile yapılmıştır)  koruyucu duvar

Alıştırma

SAYFA 88

B. Zarf + Past Participle + İsim

Past participle sıfatı, fiilden türevlendiği için zarf ile beraber kullanılabilir. Tabii, zarf sıfatı niteler ve beraberinde tercüme edilir.

Örnek:

to develop  gelişmek; developed  gelişmiş

developed system  gelişmiş sistem

well-developed system  iyi gelişmiş sistem

Alıştırma

100. Yukarıdaki açıklama ve örneğe göre, aşağıda listelenmiş zarflı past participle sıfatlarını Türkçeye çeviriniz:

a densely populated area

an over-developed muscle

an under-developed muscle

a better known fact

a little known fact

a newly-formed compound

a newly-planted tree

recently-introduced methods

well-developed roots

under-developed countries

the newly discovered species

the recently won peace

greatly reduced volume

some little-inhabited regions

greatly improved methods

an over-simplified diagram

badly managed programme

a badly-developed organ

Sözlük

compound: bileşik

densely: yoğun, sıkı bir şekilde

to develop: gelişmek, geliştirmek

to equip: donatmak

fact: hakikat, gerçek

to form: şekillenmek, oluşturmak

to improve: iyileştirmek, geliştirmek

to inhabit: iskân etmek, oturmak

to introduce: takdim etmek, uygulamaya koymak

laboratory: laboratuvar

to manage: idare etmek, yönetmek

muscle: adele, kas

over-: fazla, çok, aşırı

to plant: dikmek

peace: sulh, barış

to populate: iskân etmek, nüfuslandırmak

recently: son zamanlarda, yakınlarda

to reduce: azaltmak

root: kök

to simplify: basitleştirmek

under-: az, yetersiz, alt

volume: hacim

to win: kazanmak

XII. Participle Takımları

A. İsim + Present Participle + Edat Takımı

Açıklama

Present participle isimden sonra bir takım başında olup, gene sıfat işini görerek ismi niteler. Tercüme ederken, bu participle takımı nitelediği isimden önce yerleştirilmesi lazımdır.

Örnek:

İngilizcedeki sıra: İsim + present participle + edat takımı

the molecules moving in the gas

Türkçedeki sıra: Edat takımı + present participle + isim

gazda hareket eden moleküller

SAYFA 89

Alıştırma

101. Yukarıda geçen örnekte olduğu gibi aşağıda verilen participle takımlarını isimden önce yerleştirip Türkçeye çeviriniz:

the forests remaining in these areas

a point moving along a straight line

an organism living in the soil

a tree growing in sandy soil

a line beginning at this point

micro-organisms living in the cell

costs increasing because of scarcity of raw materials

movement continuing in waves

results differing from previous experiments.

gas escaping from the pipes

problems existing in the cotton industry

a sphere revolving at the base of the column

personnel working in modern factories

a mixture resulting from three elements

plants living in a smoky atmosphere

a disease beginning with high fever

opinions disagreeing with the majority

a disease developing from vitamin deficiency

a diet lacking in protein

waves moving in the same direction

legislation existing for the individual

a characteristic distinguishing from other species of insect

factors contributing to the general situation

a mixture consisting of sand, cement and water

a compound consisting of salt and acids

B. İsim + Present Participle + Nesne (İsim)

Present participle, fiilden türevlendiği için nesne sahibi olabilir. Yani, present participle'den sonra gelen isim onun nesnesi olup participle takımını meydana çıkarır. Yukarıda gösterilen aynı şekilde, Türkçede nitelediği isimden önce yerleştirilir.

Örnek:

İngilizcedeki sıra: İsim (1) + present participle (2) + nesnesi (3)

a liquid containing organisms

Türkçedeki sıra: Nesne (3) + present participle (2) + nitelediği isim (1)

organizmaları ihtiva eden bir sıvı

Alıştırmalar

C. İsim + Past Participle + Edat Takımı

Yukarıda present participle için gösterildiği gibi, past participle de isimden sonra takım başına gelebilir. Aynı şekilde de takip ettiği ismi niteler. Past participle anlamı edilgendir. Past participle takımı, tercümede takip ettiği isminden önce yerleştirilir.

İngilizcedeki sıra: İsim (1) + past participle (2) + edat takımı (3)

food cooked with electricity

Türkçedeki sıra: Edat takımı (3) + past participle (2) + isim (1)

elektrikle pişirilmiş yemek

Alıştırmalar

XIII. Mastar (Infinitive)

A. Fiil + Mastar

Örnek:

He wanted to learn.  Öğrenmek istedi.

SAYFA 99

İngilizcede birçok fiil mastar ile kullanılır. Türkçeye çevirirken de mastar kullanılır.

Örnek:

He prepared to go.  Gitmeye hazırlandı.

He was obliged to speak.  Konuşmak mecburiyetindeydi.

Alıştırma

107. Aşağıda verilen cümleleri örnekte gösterildiği gibi Türkçeye çeviriniz:

He was forced to answer.

They hesitated to speak.

They have learned to read.

They will begin to build.

We all wanted to know.

He was determined to go.

He agreed to pay.

They were prepared to sell.

She will attempt to explain.

They are permitted to leave.

They were invited to take part.

They like to experiment.

They intend to take part.

They refused to begin.

We wanted to understand.

They started to vibrate.

He began to argue.

We were determined to take part.

They decided to begin,

They intended to purchase.

Sözlük

to intend: niyetinde olmak, amaçlamak

to invite: davet etmek, çağırmak

to permit: müsaade etmek, izin vermek

to be prepared: hazır olmak

to purchase: satın almak

to refuse: reddetmek

to take part: iştirak etmek, katılmak

to vibrate: titremek

Olumsuz Mastar

Mastardan evvel "not" kelimesi katmakla, mastar olumsuz olur.

Örnek:

to go  gitmek / not to go  gitmemek

to forgive  affetmek / not to forgive  affetmemek

SAYFA 100

Alıştırma

108. Yukarıda 1-20 sayılı mastarlı cümlelerin mastardan önce birer "not" kelimesi ilave ederek, mastarları olumsuz yapınız. Sonra Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Örnek: 1. He was forced not to answer.  Cevap vermemeye mecbur edildi. (Not: 4, 9, 12, 15, 17 sayılı cümleleri yapmayınız).

B. Fiil + Mastar + Nesnesi

Örnek: He learned to speak the language.

Açıklama

Her geçişli fiilin mastarı bir nesne ile kullanılabilir. Nesnesi varsa, mastardan önce tercüme edilir.

Fiil + mastar + nesnesi

Örnek:

He has learned to speak French.  Fransızca konuşmayı öğrendi.

They began to read the newspaper.  Gazeteyi okumaya başladılar.

DİKKAT: Mastarın nesnesi yoksa tümleci olabilir. O da nesne gibi, mastardan önce tercüme edilir. (mastar + tümleç)

Örnek: He wants to go to England.  İngiltere'ye gitmek istiyor.

Alıştırmalar

109. Yukarıdaki açıklamaya göre ve örnekte gösterildiği gibi, aşağıda verilen nesneli mastarları bulup cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

He was forced to answer the questions.

They hesitated to speak the truth.

He has learned to read the alphabet.

We all wanted to know the result of the election.

He agreed to pay the first instalment on the goods.

They were prepared to sell the goods below the market price.

They will begin to build a new factory outside the town.

They will attempt to explain the causes of the revolution.

They are not permitted to leave the building before the end of the examination.

We wanted to understand the causes of the revolution.

They decided to begin operations next year.

They refused to begin operations before the end of the year.

They intended to purchase large supplies of wheat from U.S.S.R.

The villagers wanted to plant the seed before the spring rains.

SAYFA 101

Sözlük (Yukarıda geçen sözlüğe de bakınız.)

alphabet: alfabe

cause: sebep, neden

election: seçim

goods: eşya, mal

instalment: taksit

operations: işler, ameliyeler, operasyonlar

seed: tohum

spring: ilkbahar

revolution: devrim

truth: hakikat, gerçek

wheat: buğday

Anlama Soruları

What was he forced to answer? What was he forced to do?

What did they hesitate to speak? What did they hesitate to do?

What has he learned to read? What has he learned to do?

What did we all want to know? What did we all want to do?

What did he agree to pay? What did he agree to do?

What were they prepared to sell? What were they prepared to do?

What will they begin to build? What will they begin to do?

What will they attempt to explain? What will they attempt to do?

What are they not permitted to leave? What are they not permitted to do?

What did we want to understand? What did we want to do?

What did they decide to begin? What did they decide to do?

What did they refuse to begin? What did they refuse to do?

What did they intend to purchase? What did they intend to do?

What did the villagers want to plant? What did they want to do?

110. Yukarıda not edilmiş olan açıklamaya göre aşağıda verilen tümleçli mastarları bulup cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

They hesitated to speak to the strangers.

They were determined to go to the entrance of the valley.

They agreed to pay for the goods in dollars.

He agreed to pay in Turkish currency.

They were invited to take part in the research project.

They liked to experiment with different materials.

They intended to take part in the congress in New York.

They decided to begin with the newly-arrived strangers.

He did not want to wait for the others.

They decided to cooperate in the new research project.

Sözlük (Yukarıda geçmiş olan sözlüğe de bakınız.)

congress: kongre

to cooperate: işbirliği yapmak

currency: para, para birimi

entrance: giriş

material: malzeme

project: proje, program

research: araştırma

stranger: yabancı

valley: vadi

SAYFA 102

Anlama Soruları

In what did he agree to pay? What did he agree to do?

With what did they like to experiment? What did they like to do?

In what did they intend to take part? What did they intend to do?

With whom did they decide to begin? What did they decide to do?

For whom did he not want to wait? What did he not want to do?

111. Yukarıda verilmiş olan 1-10 cümlelerin mastarlarından önce (1, 5, 6, 9'u yapmayınız) birer "not" kelimesi ilave ederek, cümleleri olumsuz yapınız. Sonra tercüme ediniz:

Örnek:

He decided to go to England.  İngiltere'ye gitmeye karar verdi.

He decided NOT to go to England.  İngiltere'ye gitmemeye karar verdi.

112. Aşağıda verilen olumsuz mastarlı cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

They decided not to go to the meeting.

They were obliged not to agree with the decisions.

They agreed not to talk about the decisions taken.

He agreed not to leave without permission.

He decided not to work on the experiment.

They were determined not to remain in those conditions.

They decided not to be responsible for the results.

He agreed not to retire until the following year.

They tried not to cooperate with other organisations.

He decided not to carry out the proposed programme.

SAYFA 103

XIV. Strüktürel 'It' Cümlenin Öznesi

A. It + olmak fiili + sıfat + mastar

Örnek: It is easy to see.

Strüktürel "it" ile kullanılan mastar, cümlenin asıl öznesidir. Özne olan mastar da cümlenin başına alınarak tercüme edilir.

Örnek:

It was difficult to see.  Görmek zordu.

It will be easy to understand.  Anlamak kolay olacaktır.

Alıştırmalar

113. Yukarıda gösterildiği gibi, aşağıda verilen cümlelerin özne mastarlarını bulup, cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

It is important to know.

It is true to say.

It is easy to say.

It is difficult to maintain.

It was impossible to answer.

It was possible to arrange.

It will be difficult to clarify.

It would be unnecessary to arrange.

It has been impossible to find out.

It will be impossible to wait.

It is important to remember.

It is possible to produce.

It is impossible to forget.

It may be necessary to obtain.

It was difficult to accomplish.

It must be true to state.

It was easy to construct.

It may be possible to employ.

It has been difficult to discover.

It was impossible to confirm.

114. Aşağıdaki fiillere birer zarf konmuştur. Cümleleri, zarfı yerleştirerek Türkçeye çeviriniz:

It is very easy to say...

B. It ile Kullanılan Mastarın Nesnesi

It + olmak fiili + sıfat + mastar + nesnesi

Örnek: It will be easy to see the film.

Açıklama

Her geçişli fiilin mastarı, nesneye sahip olabilir. Tabii, nesnesi mastardan önce yerleştirilerek tercüme edilir.

Örnek: It was difficult to see the blackboard.  Tahtayı görmek zordu.

115. Alıştırma

It is difficult to maintain the standard.

It was never easy to construct the bridges.

It may not be possible to employ these methods.

It has sometimes been difficult to discover the real causes.

It was usually impossible to confirm the evidence.

It may not be easy to obtain enough materials.

SAYFA 106

116. Yukarıda verilmiş olan cümleler aşağıda biraz uzatılmıştır. Türkçeye çeviriniz:

It is easy to see the details of the plants in this picture.

It is important to know the cause of the confusion in the political situation.

It is difficult to maintain the standard of production of manufactured goods.

It was impossible to answer the accusations of the lawyers in the court.

Last year it was possible to arrange the new courses for English students.

It has been impossible to find out the real causes of the increase in crime in recent years both in this and other countries.

It will be difficult to clarify the situation for the visiting committee.

It may not be possible to employ these methods for the treatment of this disease in young children.

It has sometimes been difficult to discover the real causes of a war or a revolution in the history of a nation.

It was usually impossible for the defendant to confirm the evidence of his own witnesses.

It may not be easy to obtain enough materials for the new hospitals and railways in Africa.

XV. Maksat İçin Kullanılan Mastar (Infinitive of Purpose)

A. Açıklama

Mastar, maksat göstermek için kullanılır. Ancak cümlenin gelişinden anlaşılır. Türkçeye çevirirken muhakkak (için, maksadıyla veya diye) gibi bir ilave etmek doğru olur.

SAYFA 108

DİKKAT: Bu gibi cümleler iki ayrı kısımdan ibarettir. Bir kısım, maksat mastarına kadardır; öbürü, maksat mastarından sonra gelen parçadır. Bu iki kısım birbiriyle karıştırılmaksızın tercüme edilmelidir. Anlama sorularında bu iki kısım ayrı olarak belirtilmektedir.

Örnek:

He went out to buy some matches.  Kibrit almak için dışarı çıktı.

They have a machine to cut paper.  Kağıt kesmek için bir makinesi vardır.

He went to England to learn the language.  Lisan öğrenmek için İngiltere'ye gitti.

Mastarın nesnesi (varsa) mastardan evvel yerleştirilir (Sayfa 100'e bakınız).

Alıştırma

117. Aşağıda verilen cümlelerin maksat gösteren mastarlarını bulup ("için, diye, maksadıyla") gibi kelimeleri ilave ederek örnekte gösterildiği gibi cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz.

(Not: Mastarın nesnesi, tümleci (varsa) parantez içine alınmıştır. Mastardan önce yerleştiriniz.)

He bought a newspaper to read (the article on Cyprus.)

You left the room to answer (the telephone).

Larger exports are needed to pay (for the imports).

The whole text must be read to understand (it properly).

The results must be checked to find (the mistakes).

A fundamental knowledge of the structure of the language is needed to translate (the text properly).

Precautions must be taken to prevent (forest fires).

Precautions should be taken to prevent (soil erosion.)

To achieve (accurate measurements) the machine must be in good working condition.

The case was heard in private to decide (his punishment).

The markets should be studied to find (new opportunities).

Factories must be placed near the mines to keep down (the costs).

The seeds are protected to keep out (the moisture).

A high temperature is necessary to keep (the liquid hot).

The results must be recorded to prevent (mistakes).

To learn (a language) you need lots of practice.

Great care must be taken to avoid (mistakes).

Precautions should be taken to prevent (damage).

Measures will be taken to ensure (protection).

More iron and steel are needed to complete (the construction).

SAYFA 109

Sözlük

Kelime

Anlamı

Anlama Soruları

What did he do? Why did he buy a newspaper?

What did you do? Why did you leave the room?

What are needed? Why are larger exports needed?

What must be done? Why must the whole text be read?

What must be done? Why must the results be checked?

What is needed? Why is a fundamental knowledge of the structure of the language needed?

What must be done? Why must precautions be taken?

What should be done? Why should precautions be taken?

What must be in good working condition? Why must it be in good working condition?

What was done? Why was the case held in private?

What should be done? Why should the markets be studied?

What must be done? Why must factories be placed near the mines?

What must be recorded? Why must the results be recorded?

What must be done? Why must great care be taken?

What should be done? Why should precautions be taken?

What will be done? Why will measures be taken?

SAYFA 110

B. Maksat İçin Kullanılan Mastarın Nesnesi

Mastar + nesne / tümleç

Örnek: to learn the words (for the examination)  (imtihan için) kelimeleri öğrenmek maksadıyla

Açıklama

Bundan önce gelen alıştırmada parantez içine alınmış olan kelimeler, mastarın nesnesi (veya tümleci) dirler. Her geçişli mastarın nesnesi olabilir. Geçişli olmayan mastarın da tümleci olabilir. Nesne ve tümleci mastarından önce yerleştirmek en doğru tercüme yoludur.

(tümleci + nesnesi + mastar)

Örnek: He bought a dictionary to learn the words in the holidays.  Tatilde kelimeleri öğrenmek için bir lügat kitabı aldı.

Alıştırma

118. Aşağıda verilmiş olan cümleleri, örnekte gösterildiği gibi, mastarların nesnesi ve tümleci de (varsa) mastardan önce yerleştirerek Türkçeye çeviriniz:

He bought a newspaper to read the article explaining the situation in Cyprus.

The secretary left the room to answer the telephone in her office.

Larger exports are needed to pay for the import of consumer goods.

The whole text must be read to understand it properly for translation purposes.

The results of all the analyses must be checked to find the mistakes in the tables of pH values.

Precautions must be taken to prevent forest fires in dry countries, especially during the summer months.

Precautions to prevent loss of soil from erosion should be taken immediately.

To achieve accurate measurements of the pH values and exchange capacity the machine should be in good working condition.

The markets in the Far East should be studied to find new opportunities for the sale of goods manufactured in Turkey.

Iron and steel factories must be placed near the mines to keep down the cost of the transport of coal and ore.

A high temperature is necessary to keep the liquid in the top of the container at boiling point.

The results of every analysis must be recorded to prevent mistakes in the tables.

SAYFA 111

Great care must be taken to avoid mistakes in the typing of the texts.

Precautions should be taken to prevent damage from radiation.

Measures will be taken to ensure protection from the effects of radiation.

Sözlük (Yukarıda verilen sözlüğe de bakınız.)

Kelime

Anlamı

SAYFA 112

XVI. Fiil İsmi + Nesnesi (Cümlenin Öznesi Olarak - Gerund)

A. ...ing + İsim

Örnek: Learning a language is not easy.  Bir dil öğrenmek kolay değildir. (veya) Bir dilin öğrenilmesi kolay değildir.

Bu strüktürde, mastar strüktüründe olduğu gibi nesnesi, fiil isminden önce yerleştirilip tercüme edilir.

İngilizcedeki sıra: Fiil ismi (1) + nesnesi (2)

Translating a text (is difficult)

Türkçedeki sıra: Nesnesi (2) + Fiil ismi (1)

Bir metin tercüme etmek (zordur) (veya) Bir metnin tercüme edilmesi (zordur)

Alıştırma

119. Yukarıda örnekte gösterildiği gibi, aşağıda verilen özne olan ...ing fiil isminin nesnesini bulup cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Criticising the work of others is easy.

Destroying harmful insects is a long process.

Developing backward countries takes a long time.

Growing trees in poor soil is uneconomic.

Distinguishing the different species is a job for the expert.

Introducing modern methods has increased production and distribution.

Protecting the tissues from further damage is very important.

Maintaining high standards of accuracy requires effort.

Estimating cost of production is a job for the expert.

Isolating the virus is the first step towards producing a serum.

Using a concentrated solution will give better results.

Repeating vocabulary exercises is a good way to learn words.

Sözlük

Kelime

Anlamı

Kelime

Anlamı

accuracy

sıhhat, doğruluk, kesinlik

to estimate

tahmin etmek

backward

gelişmemiş, geri kalmış

exercise

alıştırma

concentrated

konsantre, yoğun

expert

uzman

to criticise

tenkid etmek, eleştirmek

harmful

zararlı

cure

tedavi

insect

böcek

damage

zarar

to isolate

tecrit etmek, izole etmek

to destroy

yok etmek

to introduce

takdim etmek, getirmek

to distinguish

tefrik etmek, ayırt etmek

job

iş

dağıtım

to maintain

muhafaza etmek, korumak

poor

SAYFA 113

process: işlem, olay, süreç

to protect: korumak

to repeat: tekrarlamak

to require: istemek, gerektirmek

solution: çözelti, solüsyon

tissue: doku

uneconomic: gayri-iktisadi, ekonomik olmayan

vocabulary: sözlük, kelime dağarcığı

Anlama Soruları

What is easy?

B. Edattan Sonra Gelen Fiil İsmi + Nesnesi

edat + ...ing + nesne

Örnek:

for + learning + a language  bir lisanı öğrenmek için / bir lisanın öğrenilmesi için

about + translating + a sentence  bir cümlenin tercümesi hakkında / bir cümlenin tercüme edilmesi hakkında

Örnekte gösterildiği gibi edatı takip eden ...ing ve nesnesi, edata tabidir ve tercümesinin iki türlüsü vardır:

for learning  öğrenmek için / öğrenilmesi için

about translating  tercüme etmek hakkında / tercüme edilmesi hakkında

Alıştırma

120. Yukarıdaki açıklama ve örneklerde olduğu gibi, aşağıda verilen (...ing ve nesne) leri edatına bağlayıp cümleleri tercüme ediniz:

This instrument is used for measuring the heights of distant clouds.

It is also used for detecting upper layers of thin clouds.

It can also be used for measuring the amount of condensation in clouds.

There has been some discussion on controlling the outflow of capital from Britain.

It is impossible to avoid the necessity for continuing control of investments.

There are no reasons for questioning the competence of the director.

SAYFA 114

This is a very reliable method of curing the infection.

These drugs are used to prevent the microbes from infecting the tissue.

This is a reliable method of measuring transpiration in plants.

The plant carries out its function of absorbing nourishment.

A rapid loss of water may be permitted by the opening of pores.

Legislation was introduced in 1911 for establishing state aid for the unemployed workers.

The government must legislate against illegal cutting in the state forests.

There is already some legislation for protecting the rights of minorities.

There are several several several several methods of isolating the virus for cultivating it in the laboratory.

Through being absent for most of the term, they missed many opportunities for learning the language.

This book contains a lot of information about collecting, preserving and classifying butterflies.

The research work is completed except for checking and comparing the results of the analyses.

Most of the workers preferred to return to work instead of going on strike.

The main functions of the organism, like breathing, feeding and reproducing, are carried out in a characteristic way.

XVII. (ON / BY / IN / WITHOUT)'dan Sonra Gelen Fiil İsmi

A. on / by / in / without + ing (nesne)

Açıklama

Aşağıda örnekte gösterildiği gibi ON / BY / IN / WITHOUT edatlarını takip eden ...ing fiil ismi özel bir anlam taşır. XVI A'da anlatıldığı gibi ...ing fiil isminin bir nesnesi de olabilir. Bilindiği gibi nesnesi, ...ing fiil isminden önce yerleştirilir.

on ...ing  ettiğinde, yapınca

by ...ing  etmekle (veya) ederek (veya) etmek suretiyle

in ...ing  etmekle (veya) etmesinde, yapmakta

without ...ing  etmeksizin (veya) etmeden

Örnekler:

on paying  ödediğinde

by cutting  kesmekle (veya) keserek (veya) kesmek suretiyle

in making  yapmakta

without speaking  konuşmaksızın (veya) konuşmadan

Nesnesi varsa:

on paying the money  parayı ödediğinde

by cutting the trees  ağaçları kesmekle, keserek, kesmek suretiyle

in making an experiment  bir deneme yapmakta

without speaking a word  tek kelime söylemeden, söylemeksizin

SAYFA 116

Alıştırma

121. Aşağıda verilen cümlelerdeki ...ing fiil ismine uygun manasını vererek örnekte olduğu gibi cümlelerini Türkçeye çeviriniz:

NOT: Görüleceği gibi, içinde bu strüktür bulunan cümleler iki kısma ayrılabilir. Bir kısım "on/by/in/without ...ing", nesnesi (varsa), tümleci (varsa); öbürü, asıl ana cümleden ibarettir. Bu iki kısmı birbirine karıştırmadan tercüme ediniz. (Anlama sorularında bu iki kısım ayrı olarak belirtilmektedir.)

By cutting the best trees, they ruined the forest.

By cutting the best trees illegally, they ruined the forests in this area.

They improved the forests by removing the diseased trees.

A scientist must prove his theory by demonstrating with experiments.

On checking the result of the experiment they saw their mistake.

In criticising their work, he pointed out their mistakes.

The result was confirmed by analysing the contents of the bottle.

By taking measures to prevent the spread of the disease, they saved many lives.

İngilizce Okuma, Anlama ve Tercüme Kılavuzu (Amok Kitabı - Bölüm 4)

Bu doküman, orijinal kaynak metnin tüm sayfalarını (Sayfa 117 - Sayfa 156) tek bir satır, sözlük kelimesi veya anlama sorusu atlanmaksızın, OCR hatalarından tamamen arındırılmış olarak sayfa sayfa içermektedir.

The crop is protected by spraying with chemicals.

The sterling area countries could cause disturbance by liquidating their balances in London.

This is a method of determining the calcium content by weighing the amount of calcium oxalate.

Fresh water is obtained by distilling sea-water.

The report cannot be finished without mentioning the results of this experiment.

In manufacturing heat-resistant glass, boric acid is used.

Trees can be protected from insect attack by applying toxic chemicals to the bark.

Working conditions are improved by introducing modern methods of air conditioning.

Plants purify the air by removing the carbon dioxide from it.

WHEN/WHILE/BEFORE/AFTER/SINCE'den Sonra Gelen Present Participle

Açıklama: when/while/before/after/since + ...ing (nesne) yapısı Türkçeye özel bir şekilde tercüme edilir:

when ...ing: ettiğinde, edince

while ...ing: ederken

before ...ing: etmeden (önce)

after ...ing: ettikten sonra

since ...ing: ettikten sonra, edeli

Örnekler:

when buying: satın aldığında, alınca

while speaking: konuşurken

before answering: cevap vermeden önce (evvel)

after completing: tamamladıktan sonra

since seeing: göreli, gördükten sonra

NOT: Present participle'ın nesnesi veya tümleci varsa, present participle'dan önce yerleştirilir.

Sayfa 119

Nesneli Örnekler:

when buying goods: eşya satın alınca

while speaking to the students: öğrencilerle konuşurken

before answering the question: soruya cevap vermeden önce

after completing the experiment: tecrübeyi tamamladıktan sonra

since seeing the pictures: resimleri göreli (gördükten sonra)

Alıştırma 122

Aşağıda verilmiş olan cümleleri iki ayrı kısım olarak tercüme ediniz:

You must think carefully before answering the question in Turkish.

After completing the experiments the results can be classified.

We can complete the research work more quickly since purchasing the new apparatus.

The sample must be weighed carefully before heating.

The sample must be weighed carefully after drying it at 150°C.

When learning a foreign language attention must be given to the structure of the sentences.

When using radio-active material, the body must be protected from the effects of radiation.

The plants developed slowly before being given extra nitrogen.

When considering the question of compensation the extent of the damage should be considered.

When considering the question of unemployment the economic development of the whole country must be taken into account.

C. When/if/unless/although/until/as/where'den Sonra Gelen Past Participle

Açıklama: Bu strüktürde kelimeler past participle'a edilgen bir anlam verir:

when: edildiğinde

if: edildiği takdirde

unless: edilmedikçe

although: edildiği halde, edilmesine rağmen

until: edilinceye kadar

as: edildiği gibi

where: edildiği yer(ler)de

Örnekler (Shown kelimesi ile):

when shown: gösterildiğinde

where shown: gösterildiği yer(ler)de

if shown: gösterildiği takdirde

unless shown: gösterilmedikçe

as shown: gösterildiği gibi

although shown: gösterildiği halde, gösterilmesine rağmen

until shown: gösterilinceye kadar

Sayfa 121

Alıştırma 123

Aşağıda verilmiş olan past participle takımlarını Türkçeleştiriniz:

1. when given | 2. if used | 3. although written | 4. until needed | 5. as guaranteed | 6. if not required | 7. unless advised | 8. although not stated | 9. where needed | 10. where planted | 11. if attacked | 12. until heated | 13. if known | 14. when cooled | 15. if needed | 16. when heated | 17. if applied | 18. when finished | 19. although guaranteed | 20. until completed | 21. although begun | 22. as expected | 23. unless completed | 24. where used | 25. unless paid for | 26. when used | 27. unless stated | 28. where proven | 29. when provided | 30. as indicated | 31. when used | 32. as mentioned | 33. as required

Alıştırma 124

When given in high concentration, some antibiotics can dissolve the walls of bacterial cells.

Fertilisers, if used in too high concentration, damage the plant.

This chemistry book, although written for students of the university, is also suitable for use in technical schools.

The rest of the samples should be kept in covered containers until needed.

This pH-metre apparatus as guaranteed by the makers, gives a high degree of accuracy.

The rest of the chemicals, if not required for immediate use, should be kept at a very low temperature in the refrigerator.

Antibiotics should not be taken as a cure unless advised by the doctor.

Although not stated in the instructions, the machine must be oiled before use.

Additional nitrogen has been added to the soil where needed.

Pine trees develop quickly where planted in sandy soils.

If attacked by disease or insects plants should be sprayed with chemicals.

The liquid does not boil until heated to 120°C.

The cause of the disease, if known, was written on the record.

When cooled, the vapour condenses and forms droplets.

The supply of oxygen may be increased if needed.

When heated the substance gives off carbon dioxide.

Antibiotics, if applied incorrectly, may be dangerous for the patient.

The building when finished, will be used as a training school.

This method was used in all experiments, unless otherwise stated.

Negligence, where proven, is punishable by law.

These insecticides must be used as indicated on the container.

When used as a cooling agent liquid nitrogen is very efficient.

As mentioned in the previous chapter, the standard of living was very low in Scotland during the seventeenth century.

The vitamin is stored in the body ready for use, as required.

XVIII Soru Kelimelerinden Sonra Gelen Mastarlar

Yapı: Soru kelimesi + mastar (to-infinitive) + (nesne) (tümleç)

Açıklama: Soru kelimesinden sonra gelen mastar, fiil isminin gelecek zamanı olarak Türkçeye çevrilir. Cümlenin kalan kısmı da bahsedilen şahsa göre bağlanır.

what to do: ne yapacağını (He told me what to do -> Bana ne yapacağımı söyledi.)

where to go: nereye gideceğini (She told you where to go -> Size nereye gideceğinizi söyledi.)

how to make: nasıl yapacağını (We showed them how to make -> Onlara nasıl yapacaklarını gösterdik.)

Mastarın nesnesi veya tümleci varsa mastardan önce tercüme edilir. Mastarın anlamı çok zaman edilgendir.

how to do the experiment: tecrübenin nasıl yapılacağını

how to translate the sentence: cümlenin nasıl tercüme edileceğini

where to put the money: paranın nereye konulacağını

where to go tomorrow: yarın nereye gidileceğini

Alıştırma 125

Aşağıda verilmiş cümle parçalarını Türkçeye çeviriniz:

1. where to build the library | 2. how to classify the viruses | 3. where to apply for work | 4. what to demonstrate to the students | 5. what to use in this experiment | 6. how to plan the work | 7. how to separate the patients | 8. how to prevent forest fires | 9. when to start work | 10. when to increase the price

Sayfa 125

11. how much water to give the plants | 12. how many students to accept | 13. which elements to mix | 14. which examination to take | 15. how much nitrogen to add | 16. which books to buy | 17. which microbes to identify | 18. how to identify the microbes | 19. which material to use | 20. how to use the material

Sayfa 128

ANLAMA VE TERCÜME İÇİN KISA METİNLER

Bu metinler C1 ve C2 düzeylerinde öğretilen cümle strüktürlerini ihtiva ederler. Metinlerde bulunan sayılar, bu eserde gösterilen strüktürlere işaret etmektedir.

1. LAW

No modern society functions without local governing bodies, elected by some or all of the citizens living in the place. Switzerland is unique among developed countries in refusing to allow women to vote. Differences arise mainly in the amount of power or initiative allowed by law or practice to any local body. In America the rights of the fifty separated states against the Federal Government are guaranteed in the constitution. Inside the states, cities and other communities govern themselves to a large extent. How much freedom can be allowed? How much centralisation of government should there be? How should a country be run efficiently without limiting too much the rights of the individual? These are questions yet not entirely answered even by experts on government and constitutional law and administration.

Strüktürler: 1. Past participle takımı, 2. Present participle takımı, 3. Past participle sıfatı, 4. Edattan sonra gelen fiil ismi, 5. Fiilden sonra gelen mastar, 6. Soru strüktürü.

2. LAW, HISTORY

The term 'democracy' originated in Ancient Greece. Up to the end of the fourth century B.C., Greece was divided into a large number of independent city states. They had developed various forms of government and constitutions at different periods of their history. With the development of systematic political thought, attempts were made to describe and classify these different sorts of government. The most natural method of distinguishing them was by asking the question 'Who rules?' Different states provided different answers to this question and different descriptive labels were correspondingly developed. In some, there was the system of aristocracy. In others, the distinguishing mark of the rulers was their wealth: this was plutocracy. Almost all the states at some stage had been under the absolute power of one man: this was tyranny. Lastly the power lay not with the monarch or small ruling class, but with the people itself: this was democracy, the rule of the "demos" or people. This was the system in Athens, for a long period the most powerful of Greek states.

Strüktürler: 1. İsim tamlaması, 2. Maksat gösteren mastar, 3. İsim fiil + nesnesi, 4. Edatından sonra gelen present participle, 5. Edilgen fiile karışan zarf, 6. Present participle sıfatı.

kudretli, güçlü

tekabül eden, karşılık gelen

to rule

hakim olmak, yönetmek

tarif eden, tanımlayıcı

hükümdar, yönetici

tiranlık, zorbalık

bulunmak, yatmak

hükümdar, kral

3. LAW, HISTORY

In 509 B. C., the Romans had banished their last king and had decided to establish a Republic. They had to reorganise the life of the State on completely new lines. Government under the King had been very simple. The King had full authority over everyone, and over all state property, and he held office for life. After the revolution, in order to prevent the power from remaining in the hands of one man, the Romans established institutions for governing, and they appointed officials to prevent each other from becoming too powerful. They made a set of rules to govern the working of the Roman state. These were unwritten, but they formed a real Constitution and they were the highest legal authority. Then they attempted to codify their law. At that time, all citizens were not equal before the law, but about 60 years later, the code of laws was applied to all citizens equally.

Strüktürler: 1. Mastar + nesnesi, 2. Maksat gösteren mastar + nesnesi, 3. Edat takımları, 4. Edattan sonra fiil ismi.

kanunname yapmak, kodlamak

4. ECONOMICS, HISTORY

More food and better transport were two essential preliminaries to the Industrial Revolution. But there were others as well. First, English land workers were free to change their jobs. They were not still tied to the land as in France or Russia. The population was growing fast. In 1700 there were five and a half million people in Britain; by 1800 there were nine million. So there was plenty of labour ready to move into the new factories and towns. Britain also had some natural advantages. To turn an agricultural society into an industrial society, power is needed. Britain had more sources of power than Holland and France. Coal became the chief source of power and Britain had plenty. Further, eighteenth century Britain had an effective central government. She was not divided into small quarrelling states like Germany and Italy. There was no violent revolution as in France in 1789. Britain was financially organised too. There were central institutions such as the Bank of England and the Stock Exchange, and these helped people to raise capital for new enterprises.

Strüktürler: 1. İsim tamlaması, 2. Mastar + nesnesi, 3. Maksat gösteren mastar, 4. Present participle sıfatı, 5. Edilgen fiile karışan zarf.
