E. Maksat ifade eden 'so that' ve 'in order that' ile başlayan zarf cümlecikleri:

so that / in order that: olması için, olsun diye, olması maksadıyla, olmak üzere

Örnek: The water was stored so that it could be used later.

Su sonradan kullanılmak üzere biriktirilmişti.

Su sonradan kullanılsın diye biriktirilmişti.

Su sonradan kullanılmak maksadıyla biriktirilmişti.

Alıştırmalar

157. a) Aşağıda verilmiş olan cümlelerdeki zarf cümleciklerini kerre içine alıp örnekte gösterildiği gibi tercüme ediniz. Sonra ana cümleciğine bağlayıp bütün cümleyi Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Costs of production must be kept to a minimum so that the annual profit may be as high as possible.

Cost of planting must be kept to a minimum so that the crop may yield an annual profit.

A number of railways have been constructed so that the hinterland may have access to the sea.

A plant must develop its various organs so that it can perform its various functions.

The root of the plant makes its way into the soil so that it can find the nourishment for the plant.

Sayfa 202

The river was brought under control so that it could be used to irrigate the land.

Through a government scheme, good seeds are raised for sale to farmers so that the quality of crop will gradually be improved.

The board of directors agreed to postpone their meeting so that members from the far east could attend.

The Bank of England and the Stock Exchange helped people to raise capital so that new enterprises could be undertaken.

It was impossible to adjust the machine so that light would fall at the required angle onto the photographic plate.

Sözlük

access: çıkış, giriş yeri, ulaşım

to adjust: ayarlamak

to agree: razı olmak, kabul etmek

angle: açı

annual: senelik, yıllık

board: heyet, kurul

cost: masraf, maliyet

planting: dikim, ekim

to construct: kurmak, inşa etmek

crop: mahsul, ürün

to develop: gelişmek, geliştirmek

enterprise: ticari iş, girişim

hinterland: iç bölge, ard ülke

to irrigate: sulamak

light: ışık

to make its way: yolunu açmak, ilerlemek

member: üye

nourishment: besin, gıda

to perform: ifa etmek, yapmak

plate: plaka, levha

to postpone: tehir etmek, ertelemek

profit: kâr, kazanç

railways: demiryolları

to raise: yetiştirmek, yükseltmek

to raise capital: sermaye sağlamak

to improve: iyileştirmek, geliştirmek

root: kök

required: lazım olan, istenilen

various: çeşitli

for sale: satış için, satılık

scheme: plan, proje

Stock Exchange: Borsa

to undertake: girişmek, başlatmak

to yield: vermek, getirmek

157. b) Şimdi aynı cümleler aşağıda 'so that' yerine 'in order that' kullanılarak yazılmıştır. Cümlelerin manası hiç de değişmiyor. Bir kere daha, bu sefer sözlüğe müracaat etmeden, Türkçeye çevirmeyi deneyiniz:

Costs of production must be kept to a minimum in order that the annual profit may be as high as possible.

Costs of planting must be kept to a minimum in order that the crop may yield an annual profit.

A number of railways have been constructed in order that the hinterland may have access to the sea.

A plant must develop its various organs in order that it may perform its various functions.

The root of the plant makes its way into the soil in order that it may find nourishment for the plant.

Sayfa 203

The river was brought under control in order that it might be used to irrigate the land.

Through a government scheme, good seeds are raised for sale to farmers in order that the quality of crop may be gradually improved.

The board of directors agreed to postpone their meeting in order that members from the far east could attend.

The Bank of England and the Stock Exchange helped people to raise capital in order that new enterprises could be undertaken.

It was impossible to adjust the machine in order that the light fall at the required angle onto the photographic plate.

Anlama soruları

A.

Why must costs of production be kept to a minimum?

Why must costs of planting be kept to a minimum?

Why have a number of railways been constructed?

Why must a plant develop its various organs?

Why does the root of the plant make its way into the soil?

Why was the river brought under control?

Why are good seeds raised for sale to farmers?

Why did the board of directors agree to postpone their meeting?

Why did the Bank of England and the Stock Exchange help people to raise capital?

In what way was it impossible to adjust the machine?

B.

What must be done so that the annual profit may be as high as possible?

What must be done so that the crop may yield an annual profit?

What has been done so that the hinterland may have access to the sea?

What must the plant do in order to perform its various functions?

What does the root of the plant do in order to find nourishment?

What was done in order to irrigate the land?

What is done in order to improve the quality of the crop?

What did the board of directors do so that members from the far east could attend?

What did the Bank of England and the Stock Exchange do so that new enterprises could be undertaken?

What was it impossible to do so that light should fall at the required angle?

Sayfa 204

F. "Netice" ifade eden zarf cümlecikleri.

Bunlar, 'with the result that' veya 'so that' ile başlar. Tercümesi şöyle olur:

with the result that / so that: neticesiyle, böylece, bunun sonucunda

Alıştırmalar

158. a) Aşağıda verilmiş bulunan cümlelerin zarf cümleciklerini ayırdıktan sonra, kalan ana cümleye bağlayıp tümünü Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The brain filters information so that only some aspects are important at any one time.

A break in a bone is followed by great activity of the bone cells, so that the gap is closed by new bone within a few weeks.

Illegal cutting of trees has ruined large areas of forest so that there is no longer enough wood for the needs of the building industry.

Different minerals have different rates of expansion so that, with nightly cooling, rocks begin to break off in layers.

The water in the cracks of the rocks freezes and expands so that the crack is widened.

There is a rapid increase in temperature towards the centre of the earth so that in a deep mine it is unbearably hot.

The magma is squeezed into the core of mountain ranges so that millions of years afterwards, this core is exposed.

The river deepens and widens its own valley so that the valley has a typical V section with unstable banks.

In the lower stretches the river valley has a broad open section so that the erosive power is limited.

The rain gradually washes the salt out of the soil so that fresh-water marshes replace salt marshes.

Sözlük

activity: faaliyet

any one time: muayyen bir zaman, herhangi bir zaman

aspect: yön, cephe, bakış açısı

bank: kenar, kıyı, nehir kenarı

bone: kemik

brain: beyin

break: kırık

to break off: kopmak, parçalara ayrılmak

building: bina, yapı

cell: hücre

centre: merkez

to close: kapatmak, kapanmak

cooling: soğuma

core: iç, çekirdek, öz

crack: çatlak

cutting: kesim, kesme

to deepen: derinleştirmek

erosive: aşındırıcı

to expand: genişlemek, genleşmek

expansion: genişleme, genleşme

to expose: açığa çıkarmak, maruz bırakmak

to filter: süzmek, filtrelemek

to freeze: donmak

fresh water: tatlı su

gap: boşluk, açık

gradually: yavaş yavaş, kademeli olarak

illegal: gayri-meşru, yasa dışı

Sayfa 205

layer: tabaka, katman

to limit: tahdit etmek, sınırlamak

no longer: artık ... (olumsuz)

marsh: bataklık

mine: ocak, maden ocağı

range: sıra (dağlar)

rapid: hızlı, süratli

rate: oran, hız, sürat

to replace: yerine geçmek, yenisiyle değiştirmek

rock: kaya

to ruin: mahvetmek, yok etmek

section: kesit, bölüm

stretch: bölüm, geçtiği yer

to squeeze: sıkıştırmak, fışkırtmak

unbearably: dayanılmaz derecede

to widen: genişletmek

158. b) Bu sefer aynı cümleler 'so that' yerine 'with the result that' kullanılarak aşağıda verilmiştir. Cümlelerin manası değişmiyor. Aynı şekilde, sözlüğe müracaat etmeden Türkçeye çevirmeyi deneyiniz:

The brain filters information with the result that only some aspects are important at any one time.

A break in a bone is followed by great activity of the bone cells, with the result that the gap is closed within a few weeks.

Illegal cutting of trees has ruined large areas of forest with the result that there is no longer enough wood for the needs of the building industry.

Different minerals have different rates of expansion with the result that with nightly cooling, rocks begin to break off in layers.

The water in the cracks of the rocks freezes and expands with the result that the crack is widened.

There is a rapid increase in temperature towards the centre of the earth with the result that in a deep mine it is unbearably hot.

The magma is squeezed into the core of mountain ranges with the result that millions of years afterwards, this core is exposed.

The river deepens and widens its own valley with the result that the valley has a typical V section with unstable banks.

In the lower stretches, the river valley has a broad open section with the result that the erosive power of the water is limited.

The rain gradually washes the salt out of the soil with the result that fresh-water marshes replace salt marshes.

Anlama soruları

A.

With what result does the brain filter information?

With what result is a break in a bone be followed by great activity of the bone cells?

With what result has illegal cutting of trees ruined large areas of forest?

Sayfa 206

With what result have different minerals different rates of expansion?

With what result does the water in the cracks freeze and expand?

With what result is there a rapid increase in temperature towards the centre of the earth?

With what result is the magma squeezed into the core of the mountain ranges?

With what result does the river deepen and widen its own valley?

With what result has the river valley a broad open section in the lower stretches?

With what result does the rain gradually wash the salt out of the soil?

B.

What does the brain do?

What follows a break in a bone?

What has ruined large areas of forest?

What have different minerals?

What freezes and expands?

Where is there a rapid increase in temperature?

Where is the magma squeezed?

What does the river do?

Where has the valley a broad open section?

What does the rain gradually do?

G. Şart ifade eden zarf cümlecikleri

a) 'if', 'provided that', 'on condition that' en mühim işaret kelimeleridir. Tercümesi şöyle olur:

if, provided that, on condition that: eğer / şayet, ... şartıyla

b) 'unless' bunlara benzer bir mana taşır, yalnız fiili olumsuz kılar.

Örnek:

if he comes: (eğer) (şayet) gelirse

unless he comes: (eğer) (şayet) gelmezse

if the plant dies: (eğer) (şayet) bitki ölürse

unless the plant dies: (eğer) (şayet) bitki ölmezse / ölmedikçe

provided that the money is paid: (eğer) (şayet) para ödenirse / ödenmesi şartıyla

unless the money is paid: (eğer) (şayet) para ödenmezse

on condition that the work is done: işin yapılması şartıyla

unless the work is done: (eğer) (şayet) iş yapılmazsa / yapılmadıkça

Aslında İngilizcede üç türlü şart cümlesi vardır:

Tip

Zaman

Örnek

Açıklama

I

Şimdiki veya gelecek zaman

If you ring the bell, the door will open.

Zili çalarsanız kapı açılır (açılacak) - Basit şekil

II

Geçmiş zaman

If you rang the bell, the door would open.

Zili çalınca kapı açılırdı

III

Past perfect zamanı

If you had rung the bell, the door would have opened.

Zili çalmış olsaydınız (çalsaydınız) kapı açılacaktı (açılırdı) - Şart yerine getirilmiyor

Bu eser, teknik ve bilimsel metinlerin okunmasına bir hazırlık olduğu için, sadece birinci şekil (Type I) ele alınmıştır. Öteki şekillere bu cins metinlerde az rastlanır. Alıştırmalarda yalnız basit şartlı cümleler kullanılmıştır. Bazılarında ana cümle, zarf cümleciğinden sonra, bazılarında ondan önce yerleştirilmiştir.

Alıştırmalar

160. Aşağıda yazılan 'if' ile başlayan zarf cümleciklerini Türkçeye çeviriniz:

if the microbes are examined under a microscope

161. Aşağıda bulunan cümlelerdeki şart zarf cümleciklerini kerre içine alıp tercüme ettikten sonra kalan ana cümlelere bağlayıp tümünü Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Certain mineral salts are necessary if the plant is to grow normally.

If we want to influence the growth of an animal we must study the effects of different feeding regimes.

If we think of living organisms as a State, then the DNA represents its constitution, since it lays down the laws of the state's life and development.

Some of the differences between animals can be more clearly understood if one understands their evolutionary history.

If a star shines as brightly as the sun then its distance can be measured from its apparent brightness.

For a very distant galaxy, the visible light will be observed as infra-red radiation, if it can penetrate the earth's atmosphere.

If we measure the radio-active components in some of the very old rocks, we get an idea of their age.

If the committee has fixed the wages, and if the Ministry has accepted their recommendations, no one can pay less or more.

Each living species will multiply and spread if the conditions are favourable.

If each worker's total production is low the country will be poor.

If it is treated early and by modern methods, tuberculosis can readily be cured.

It is useless to provide more land for crops if the villagers are too weak from disease to do the extra work required.

If all the food in the world is shared among total population, no-one will get enough to eat.

If a large area of land is cleared of trees and farmed badly the fertile top soil will rapidly become desert.

Sayfa 209

If erosion is allowed to continue, good farm land will rapidly become desert. Demonstration farms can be started in many countries only if generous help is supplied from advanced countries.

If a sample of well-cultivated soil is taken and pressed tightly into a jar the crumb structure is not destroyed, but if it is heated and dried, the crumb structure is destroyed.

If oxidation is too rapid the soil may be made sterile.

If the costs of production can be kept to a minimum the annual profit will be high.

If there is any possibility of cancer, or if the gastric ulcer has relapsed within a year of healing, surgery should be considered.

If the patient is overweight, his diet should be restricted. If he is underweight, or if dieting is not successful, oral anti-diabetic therapy may be recommended.

Sözlük

to accept: kabul etmek

advanced: ilerlemiş, gelişmiş

age: yaş

to allow: müsaade etmek, izin vermek

atmosphere: atmosfer

certain: muayyen, belirli

to clear: temizlemek

component: bileşen

to consider: düşünmek, dikkate almak

Anlama soruları

A.

When are certain mineral salts necessary?

When must we study the effects of different feeding regimes?

In which circumstance does DNA represent its constitution?

When can some of the differences between animals be more clearly understood?

When can a star's distance be measured from its apparent brightness?

When will the visible light be observed as infra-red radiation?

In what circumstances can we get an idea of the age of some very old rocks?

In which two circumstances can no-one pay less or more?

In what circumstances will each living organism multiply and spread?

When will the country be poor?

When can tuberculosis be readily cured?

When is it useless to provide more land for crops?

In what circumstances will no-one get enough to eat?

In which circumstances will the fertile top-soil be washed away? When will good farm land rapidly become desert?

Only when can demonstration farms be started in many countries?

When is the crumb structure not destroyed? When is it destroyed?

In what circumstance may the soil be made sterile?

On what condition will annual profit be high?

In which two circumstances should surgery be considered?

When should the patient's diet be restricted? When may oral anti-diabetic therapy be recommended?

Sayfa 211

B.

What are necessary if the plant is to grow normally?

What must we do if we want to influence the growth of an animal?

What does DNA represent? What does DNA lay down?

What can be understood more clearly?

From what can a star's distance be measured?

What will be observed as infra-red radiation?

What do we get if we measure the radio-active components in old rocks?

What can no-one do, if wages are fixed by the committee?

What will each living organism do if conditions are favourable?

If each worker's total production is low what will happen?

What can readily be cured with early treatment and modern methods?

What is it useless to do if the villagers are too weak from disease?

If all the food in the world is shared among the total population, what will happen?

What will happen to the top-soil if a large area of land is badly farmed? What will good farmland rapidly become?

What can be started in many countries?

What happens if the soil sample is heated and dried?

What may be made sterile if oxidation is too rapid?

What will be high if the costs of production can be kept to a minimum?

What should be considered if the ulcer has relapsed?

What should be restricted for an overweight patient? What should be done if dieting is not successful?

provided that

162. Aynı yukarıdaki gibi, cümlecikleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Provided that mineral salts, water, light and carbon dioxide are present, a plant will grow normally.

Provided that one understands the evolutionary history, the differences between animals can be clearly understood.

The distance of a star can be measured from its apparent brightness provided that it shines as brightly as the sun.

Provided that the committee has fixed the wages and on condition that the Ministry has accepted their recommendations, no-one can pay less or more.

Each living organism will multiply and spread provided that the conditions are favourable.

Tuberculosis can readily be cured provided that it is treated early and by modern methods.

Provided that it is neither heated nor dried, the crumb structure of a well-cultivated soil will not be destroyed.

The annual profit will be higher provided that costs of production are kept to a minimum.

(Yukarıdaki sözlüğe bakınız.)

Sayfa 212

Anlama soruları

A.

In what circumstances will a plant grow normally?

When can the differences between animals be clearly understood?

In what circumstance can the distance of a star be measured from its apparent brightness?

In which two circumstances can no-one pay less or more?

When will each living organism multiply and spread?

On what condition can tuberculosis be cured readily?

When will the crumb structure of a well-cultivated soil not be destroyed?

When will the annual profit be higher?

b) Unless

Alıştırmalar

163. Aşağıda verilmiş 'unless' ile başlayan zarf cümleciklerini Türkçeye çeviriniz.

NOT: Önceki verilmiş açıklamaya bakınız (sayfa 206). 'Unless' kelimesi fiili olumsuz kılar.

Örnek: Unless the money is paid -> para ödenmezse

unless plenty of water is given

unless the substance is heated rapidly

unless a varied diet is given

unless the rainfall is very high

unless guilt is proved beyond reasonable doubt

unless it is destroyed

unless atmospheric nitrogen is combined with other chemical elements

unless the disease is diagnosed and treated as early as possible

unless a reasonable standard of living can be guaranteed for all workers

unless better methods of farming are used in the underdeveloped countries

unless the world's food supply can be greatly increased within the next 20 years

unless the ulcer has healed completely

Sözlük

to combine: birleştirmek

completely: tamamen

to diagnose: teşhis etmek

diet: perhiz, gıda, diyet

doubt: şüphe

to heal: kapanmak (yara), iyileşmek

guilt: suçluluk

plenty: bol, çok

rainfall: yağış, yağış miktarı

rapidly: süratli, hızlıca

reasonable: makul, akla uygun

standard: seviye, standart

supply: stok, miktar, arz, tedarik

underdeveloped: gelişmemiş

varied: çeşitli, çeşitlendirilmiş

Sayfa 213

164. Aşağıda bulunan cümlelerin 'unless' kelimesiyle başlayan cümleciğini kerre içine alıp, fiilini olumsuz şekle koyunuz. Sonra ana cümleye bağlayarak tümünü Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Unless microbes are infected with a particular bacterial virus, no toxin is produced.

Unless food production can be increased rapidly a large number of the population will die of hunger.

Unless the increase in population can be checked large numbers of people will die of hunger.

We can see nothing of the tiny life around us unless we use a microscope.

Meat remains free from decay unless microbes are present.

Unless our food contains a sufficient quantity of essential substances, the body does not function efficiently.

It is useless to clear a district of malaria unless the work is maintained later.

Unless certain mineral salts are available, the plant cannot grow normally.

A country cannot be prosperous unless each worker's total production is high.

The bank would not employ any male worker unless he had completed his national service.

Unless costs of production are kept low there can be only a very small profit.

Photosynthesis cannot take place unless light has access to the leaves.

In sandy soils unless there is an underlying layer of clay, water may drain away too rapidly.

Unless a number of railways are constructed, the hinterland will have no access to the sea.

Sözlük

to have access: varabilmek, erişebilmek

annual: yıllık, senelik

available: mevcut, hazır, eldeki

certain: muayyen, belirli

to check: durdurmak, kontrol etmek

clay: kil

to clear: temizlemek

to complete: tamamlamak

to construct: yapmak, döşemek, inşa etmek

to contain: ihtiva etmek, içermek

decay: çürümek, bozulma

district: bölge

to drain away: süzülüp gitmek

efficiently: iyi bir şekilde, verimle

to employ: iş vermek, kullanmak

essential: elzem, tam gerekli

free from: ...siz, ...suz, -den ari

to function: işlemek, çalışmak

hinterland: denizden uzak olan kara, ard ülke

to increase: artırmak, çoğalmak

to be infected with: bulaşmış olmak

layer: tabaka, katman

to maintain: devam ettirmek, sürdürmek

malaria: sıtma

male: erkek

national service: askerlik

Sayfa 214

a particular: muayyen bir, özel bir

photosynthesis: fotosentez

to produce: hasıl etmek, üretmek

production: üretim

profit: kâr, kazanç

prosperous: refahlı, zengin

to remain: kalmak

sandy: kumlu

sufficient: yeter, yeterli

to take place: vuku bulmak, olmak

tiny: ufacık, çok küçük

total: tüm, bütün, toplam

Anlama soruları

A.

When is no toxin produced?

When will a large number of people die of hunger?

When will large numbers of people die of hunger?

When can we see nothing of the tiny life around us?

When does meat remain free from decay?

When does the body not function properly?

When is it useless to clear an area of malaria?

When cannot the plant grow normally?

When cannot a country be prosperous?

When would the bank not employ any male worker?

When can there be only a very small profit?

When cannot photosynthesis take place?

When may water drain away too rapidly?

When will the hinterland have no access to the sea?

B.

If microbes are not infected with a particular bacterial virus, what is not produced?

If food production cannot be increased rapidly what will happen?

If the increase in population cannot be checked, what will happen?

If we do not use a microscope, what can we not see?

If no microbes are present what happens to meat?

If our food does not contain a sufficient quantity of essential substances what happens?

Unless the work is maintained later, what is useless?

Unless certain mineral salts are available, what cannot happen?

Unless each worker's total production is high, what cannot happen?

If he had not completed his national service, what would the bank not do?

Unless costs of production are kept low, what can there be?

Unless light has access to the leaves what cannot take place?

In sandy soils unless there is an underlying layer of clay, what may happen?

Unless a number of railways are constructed, what will happen?

Sayfa 215

MUKAYESE STRÜKTÜRLERİ

A. En basit mukayese strüktürü 'than' kelimesi kullanmadan, bir tek fikirden ibarettir.

Sıfatına veya zarfına '...er' takısı veya 'more' kelimesi katılır. Türkçe manası 'daha' kelimesiyle ifade edilir.

Örnek:

big (büyük) -> bigger (daha büyük)

soft (yumuşak) -> softer (daha yumuşak)

dry (kuru) -> drier (daha kuru)

clearly (açık bir şekilde) -> more clearly (daha açık bir şekilde)

readily (kolay bir şekilde) -> more readily (daha kolay bir şekilde)

slowly (yavaşça) -> more slowly (daha yavaşça)

intelligent (zeki) -> more intelligent (daha zeki)

complicated (karışık) -> more complicated (daha karışık)

NOT: Aşağıda verilen bir kaç örneğe dikkat edip öğreniniz:

much more, far more: çok daha çok

many more: daha bir çok

a little more: biraz daha (çok)

less: daha az

much less, far less: çok daha az

a little less: biraz daha az

165. Bunlar aşağıda bir cümle parçası olarak gösterilmiştir. Tercüme ediniz:

There is much more light here.

This problem is much more difficult.

There are many more students now.

He bought many more books today.

You gave me less food today.

This time less work was done.

You gave me much less food today.

This time much less work was done.

He wanted a little more information.

He must pay a little more money.

He paid a little less money.

Give him a little less meat.

166. Aşağıdaki cümlelerin mukayese şeklinde kullanılan sıfatı (veya zarfı) bulup altını çiziniz. Sonra cümleyi Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Certain individuals may have a greater resistance to disease.

DNA is a chemical, like sulphuric acid, only it is much more complex.

[Metinde atlanmış numara]

In Lowland Britain, the environment is kinder, and the soil is richer and deeper.

The rocks underlying the lowlands are younger in the geological sense.

Sayfa 216

The rocks are softer and less resistant to erosion.

In the lowlands of eastern Britain under drier conditions there is a narrower margin between precipitation and evaporation.

Loamy soils contain a smaller percentage of sand and a higher percentage of silt and clay.

The better soils are cultivated, the poorer soils have remained uncultivated woodland or rough grazing.

People in cold climates need more fat in their diet.

In tropical countries there is a greater danger of infection.

In a temperate climate there is less danger of infection.

Vegetation grows more richly in the rain forests near the equator.

A river cuts out its bed at a slower rate on a gentle slope.

A river cuts out its bed much fast on a steep slope.

The evaporation takes place more quickly at a higher temperature.

Roots absorb much less water in cold weather.

The tree limit is much higher in hot climates.

When the substance is heated the molecules move faster.

Higher or lower wages cannot be paid if the government has fixed the prices.

Sözlük

bed: yatak (nehir yatağı)

certain: muayyen, belirli

clay: kil

climate: iklim

complex: muğlak, komplike, karmaşık

to cultivate: işlemek

detail: ayrıntı, detay

diet: perhiz, diyet

environment: çevre, muhit

equator: ekvator

evaporation: buharlaşma

fat: yağ

to fix: tespit etmek

gentle: hafif, yumuşak, az (meyil)

grazing: otlatma, otlaklık

to heat: ısıtmak

individual: fert, şahıs

kind: kibar, iyi, elverişli

limit: sınır, hudut

loamy: balçıklı, killi ve kumlu toprak

lowland: düzlük, ova

map: harita

margin: fark, hudut, pay

narrow: dar

percentage: yüzdesi

precipitation: yağış

price: fiyat

rate: hız, sürat, oran

resistance: mukavemet, direnç

resistant: mukavemetli, dirençli

richly: bol, zengin bir şekilde

scale: mikyas, ölçek

sense: mana, anlam

silt: mil, alüvyon

slope: meyil, yokuş, yamaç

steep: dik

to take place: vuku bulmak, meydana gelmek

wages: ücret

woodland: ağaçlık, ormanlık alan

Anlama soruları

What may certain individuals have?

Which is more complex, the chemical DNA or sulphuric acid?

What does a map with a large scale do?

Sayfa 217

What is the environment like in Lowland Britain? And what is the soil like?

What are the rocks underlying the lowlands like?

What are the rocks like?

What is there between precipitation and evaporation in the lowlands of eastern Britain?

What two things do loamy soils contain?

Which soils are cultivated? Which soils have remained uncultivated?

What do people in cold climates need in their diet?

What is there in tropical countries?

What is there in a temperate climate?

How does vegetation grow in the rain forests near the equator?

How does a river cut out its bed on a gentle slope?

How does a river cut out its bed on a steep slope?

How does evaporation take place at a higher temperature?

What do roots absorb in cold weather?

What is the tree limit in hot climates?

How do the molecules move when the substance is heated?

What cannot be paid if the government has fixed the prices?

B. 'Than' kelimesi kullanan mukayese strüktürleri

Bunlardan 3 türlü vardır:

a) 'than'dan sonra gelen fiil yazılmaz, ilk gelen fiilin aynısı olduğu için yazılmadan anlaşılır.

Örnek: Ahmet is taller than you. (you are anlaşılır) -> Ahmet senden uzun boyludur.

b) 'than'dan sonra gelen fiil yazılır.

Örnek: Ahmet is younger than he looks. -> Ahmet göründüğünden daha gençtir.

c) 'than'dan sonra gelen fiil, ilk gelen fiilin aynısıdır; tekrarlamamak için, yerine 'do, does veya did' kullanılır.

Örnek: Ahmet came back earlier than he did last week. ('did' fiili 'came back' yerinde kullanılmıştır) -> Ahmet geçen haftadakinden daha erken döndü.

Şimdi yukarıda açıklanan bu üç türlü mukayese strüktürleri için aşağıda birer alıştırma verilmiştir. Her cümlede 'than'dan sonra gelip mukayese edilen şeyi tespit etmek faydalı olur. Türkçeye çevirmek için bu iki şey yan yana getirilir.

Alıştırma

167. a) 'than'dan sonra gelen fiil yazılmaz, anlaşılır:

Corsican pine grows more slowly than Scotch pine.

Sayfa 218

People in cold climates need more fats than those in warm climates.

Silk is a better insulator than cotton.

The large-scale map shows more detail than the small-scale one.

Humus contributes more than any other substance to the fertility of the soil.

Spain produces more olive oil than any other country.

War, accident and old age kill much fewer people than starvation and disease.

The genetic code is much more complex than the Morse code.

Man and monkeys have more acute vision than most other animals.

Between 1939 and 1945 more lives were lost from lack of food than by all the bombs and bullets of the war.

Nowadays we tend to think more of liberty than of responsibility.

A crowd is emotionally less under voluntary control than an individual.

Stars 1000 times brighter than the sun amount to fewer than 0.01 percent of all the stars in space.

Stars brighter than the sun represent fewer than 7 per cent of the star population in our solar neighbourhood.

Stars 10,000 times fainter than the sun are more numerous than stars 100 times brighter than the sun.

Sözlük

acute: keskin

to amount to: sayısı ... bulmak, ... miktarına ulaşmak

bright: parlak

bullet: kurşun

climate: iklim

complex: muğlak, komplike, karmaşık

to contribute: yardım etmek, katkıda bulunmak

corsican pine: kara çam

crowd: kalabalık

detail: ayrıntı, detay

faint: soluk, sönük

fat: yağ

fertility: verimlilik

individual: fert, şahıs

insulator: izolatör, yalıtkan

lack: eksiklik, yokluk

liberty: hürriyet, özgürlük

neighbourhood: çevre, yakınlık, civar

numerous: çok, sayısı çok

olive oil: zeytin yağı

responsibility: sorumluluk

scale: mikyas, ölçek

scotch pine: sarı çam

silk: ipek

space: uzay, boşluk

starvation: açlık, açlıktan ölme

voluntary: ihtiyari, gönüllü

vision: görme kabiliyeti, görüş

Anlama soruları

Which grows more slowly, Corsican or Scotch pine?

Who need more fats, people in cold climates or in warm?

Which is a better insulator, silk or cotton?

Which shows more detail, the large-scale or the small-scale map?

What does humus contribute?

Sayfa 219

Which kill fewer people, war, accident and old age or starvation and disease?

What does Spain produce?

Which is more complex, the genetic code or the Morse code?

What have man and monkeys?

Between 1939 and 1945 how were more lives lost, from lack of food or by all the bombs and bullets of the war?

What do we tend to think of more nowadays, liberty or responsibility?

Which is less under voluntary control, a crowd or an individual?

What amount to fewer than 0.01 per cent of all the stars in space?

What represent fewer than 7 percent of the star population in our solar neighbourhood?

Which are more numerous, stars 10,000 times fainter or 100 times brighter than the sun?

b) 'than' dan sonra gelen fiil yazılır.

Alıştırma

167. b): Her cümlede 'than' dan sonra yazılan ikinci fiil bulunur. Mukayese edilen iki şeyi de tespit ettikten sonra, Türkçeye çeviriniz:

We have more intelligence than we need to use.

In Britain as a whole, more land is being gained at present than is being lost.

Two thousand years ago the city of Tunis was of more importance than it is today.

[Yer değiştirmiş veya orijinal metne göre 3. cümle aşağıya kaymış] Laser light can be concentrated upon a far object to a degree millions of times greater than that achieved by a good searchlight.

More people lost their lives between 1939 and 1945 from starvation and disease than were killed by the bullets and bombs of the war.

Nowadays we tend to think more of liberty than we appreciate responsibility.

Social problems of today present greater difficulty to man than those he had to face two hundred years ago.

Bacteria can grow more quickly in diseased wood than they can in healthy wood.

Sözlük

to appreciate: takdir etmek

bullet: kurşun

to concentrate: konsantre olmak, yoğunlaşmak

degree: derece

difficulty: zorluk, müşkülat

diseased: hastalıklı

to face: karşılaşmak, yüz yüze gelmek

to gain: kazanmak

healthy: sağlam, sıhhatli, sağlıklı

intelligence: zekâ

liberty: hürriyet, özgürlük

to present: arz etmek, sunmak

responsibility: sorumluluk

searchlight: projektör, ışıldak

to tend: meyil etmek, yönelmek

as a whole: bütün olarak

Sayfa 220

Anlama soruları

What have we?

In Britain as a whole what is being gained?

To what degree can laser light be concentrated on a far object?

What was the city of Tunis two thousand years ago?

What killed more people between 1939 and 1945?

What do we tend to do nowadays more than we appreciate responsibility?

What do social problems of today do?

What do bacteria grow in more quickly, healthy or diseased wood?

c) 'than' dan sonra gelen fiil 'do, does veya did' olur.

Alıştırma

168. c) Her cümlede 'than'dan sonra gelen 'do, does, did' fiilinin hangi fiilin yerine kullanıldığını tespit ediniz. İki mukayese edilen şeyi bulduktan sonra, cümleyi Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Nowadays we tend to think more of liberty than we do of responsibility.

If the experiment is repeated you will obtain better results than you did last time.

These problems do not present more difficulty than they did before.

The body absorbs sugar more quickly than it does fats.

Water boils more quickly at high altitudes than it does at sea-level.

Bacteria find rotten wood more suitable for their growth than they do healthy wood.

The report took longer to prepare than it did last year.

Trees grow at a higher level in hot climates than they do in cold.

Evaporation takes place faster at a high temperature than it does at a low.

All bodies weigh about six times less on the moon than they do on the earth.

Sözlük

altitude: irtifa, yükseklik

body: cisim, varlık, vücut

to boil: kaynamak

climate: iklim

evaporation: buharlaşma

fat: yağ

healthy: sağlam, sıhhatli

level: seviye

liberty: hürriyet

to obtain: elde etmek

to prepare: hazırlamak

to present: arz etmek, sunmak

to repeat: tekrarlamak

responsibility: sorumluluk

rotten: çürük

suitable: uygun

to tend: meyil etmek

to weigh: ağırlığı olmak, tartılmak

Sayfa 221

Anlama soruları

C. 'As ... as' ve 'the same ... as' mukayese strüktürleri

as ... as / the same ... as: kadar, gibi, aynı ...

Mukayese edilen iki şeyi tespit etmek faydalıdır.

Örnek:

A car cannot travel as fast as an aeroplane. -> Otomobil, uçak kadar hızlı gidemez.

The railway follows the same valley as the river. -> Demiryolu, nehrin takip ettiği vadiyi takip ediyor. (Demiryolu, nehir gibi aynı vadiyi takip ediyor.)

Ahmet is not as old as he looks. -> Ahmet, göründüğü kadar yaşlı değildir.

Alıştırma

169. Aşağıda verilen cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

A living organism as simple as a bacterium contains several thousand different protein molecules.

Old Red Sandstone beds were laid down in fresh water lakes at the same time as the marine beds of Devonian.

The Sahara desert is almost as large as the continent of Europe.

Pure iron is not as strong as its alloys.

When a liquid is cold the molecules do not move as fast as they do when it is heated.

A telescope as large as the one in California has never been constructed before.

Two hundred years ago the town was not as important nor as big as it is today.

One individual does not have the same innate resistance to disease as another.

Corsican pine does not grow at the same rate as Scotch pine.

People in warm climates do not require as much fat in their diet as people in cold climates.

Sayfa 222

No other country produces as much olive oil as Spain.

There is not the same danger of infection from cholera in cold climates as there is in the tropics.

The root system of a plant does not absorb as much water during cold weather as it does in warmer temperatures.

In cold climates the tree-limit is not as high as it is in tropical countries.

The small scale map does not show as much detail as the large scale one.

War, accident and old age do not kill as many people each year as disease and starvation.

Before the use of disinfectants, at least as many soldiers died of infection after the battle as were killed on the battlefield.

Cotton is not as good an insulator as wool or silk.

Heredity is just as important a factor in development as environment.

Fire-engines do not need to be brought as close to the fire as they did before pipes were used to carry water.

There are twice as many people in Europe as there are in North and South America together.

Few animals have been able to develop as acute vision as man and monkeys.

Sözlük

alloy: alaşım

Lincoln/Battlefield: savaş meydanı

to construct: inşa etmek

Anlama soruları

III. SIFAT CÜMLECİĞİ (RELATIVE CLAUSE)

Sıfat cümleciği bir ismi niteler. İngilizcede nitelediği isimden sonra gelir. Türkçede o isimden önce gelir.

İşaret kelimeleri şunlardır:

where, who, whom, whose, which, that

Yukarıda gösterilen her işaret kelimesi için aşağıda alıştırmalar verilmiştir.

NOT: 'THAT' işaret kelimesi 'WHICH', 'WHO' ve 'WHOM' işaret kelimelerinin yerine kullanılabilir. Anlamda hiçbir fark teşkil etmez.

Alıştırmalar

a) WHO - olan, olduğu, olmuş olduğu

170. Aşağıda verilen sıfat cümleciklerini, nitelediği isimden önce yerleştirerek Türkçeye çeviriniz:

employers who pay insurance

people who are involved in accidents

businessmen who have invested capital

individuals who belong to a group

an individual who commits a crime

Sayfa 224

employees who receive payment

an employee who is dismissed

an author who expresses his opinions

a dictator who wishes to remain in power

children who were employed in industry

a child who comes from a good home and receives a good education

a person who may later become a leader

parents who have more than one child

anyone who accepts this idea

a majority who have the right to vote

a few people who have no right to vote

someone who cannot understand this principle

everyone who receives the protection of society

students who may be mentally immature

everyone who receives insurance benefits

scientists who have tried to explain this idea

a manufacturer who produces cheap goods for markets in the Far East

Sözlük

to accept: kabul etmek

author: yazar

benefit: fayda, yarar

to commit: icra etmek, işlemek (suç)

crime: suç

to be dismissed: işten çıkarılmak, yol verilmek

education: tahsil, eğitim

to employ: iş vermek, çalıştırmak

employee: işçi, çalışan

employer: işveren

to express: ifade etmek

immature: olgun değil, ham

individual: şahıs, fert, kişi

insurance: sigorta

to invest: para yatırmak, yatırım yapmak

to be involved in: maruz kalmak, uğramak, karışmak

majority: çoğunluk

manufacturer: fabrikatör, üretici

market: piyasa, pazar

mentally: zihnen, zihinsel olarak

opinion: fikir, kanaat

in power: iktidarda, hakim kudrette

principle: prensip, ilke

to produce: imal etmek, üretmek

protection: korunma, koruma

to receive: almak

right: hak

to vote: oy kullanmak

171. Aşağıda verilen cümledeki 'who' ile başlayan sıfat cümleciğini kerre içine alıp nitelediği isimden önce yerleştiriniz. Sonra cümleyi Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The blood of a man who is healthy may be injected into the veins of a man who is suffering from anaemia.

There are many enlightened farmers who are ready to experiment with new and better ways of growing food.

Two thirds of all the men, women and children who live on the earth today spend their lives in poverty.

New villages have been built to provide homes for the families who are making a living on the land.

Sayfa 225

Society can be divided into three classes: the few who make things happen; the many who watch things happen and the great majority who have no idea of what happens (olup bitenler).

Brillouin, who expanded Einstein's ideas, gave us an idea of the frequency of components of scattered light.

William Smith, who has rightly been called the Father of English Geology, found different specimens of fossils of the same species in different parts of the country.

Another division in society is between the few who own or control the machine and the mass who have only the ability to work.

Sözlük

ability: kabiliyet, yetenek

anaemia: kansızlık, anemi

to call: isimlendirmek, adlandırmak

component: bileşen

to divide: bölmek

division: bölme, bölünme

enlightened: aydın, bilgili

to expand: genişletmek, büyütmek

frequency: frekans, sıklık

to make a living: hayat kazanmak, geçinmek

to own: sahip olmak

poverty: sefalet, yokluk, fakirlik

to provide: sağlamak, temin etmek

rightly: haklı olarak

scattered: difüz, yayılmış, saçılmış

mass: kütle, yığın

to inject: zerk etmek, enjekte etmek

species: tür

to suffer from: ... hastası olmak, -den muzdarip olmak

two thirds: üçte ikisi

vein: damar

to watch: seyretmek, izlemek

way: usul, metot, yol

Anlama soruları

A.

Whose blood may be injected into whose veins?

What kind of enlightened farmers are there?

Who spend their lives in poverty?

For which families have the new villages been built?

Into which three classes can society be divided?

Who expanded Einstein's ideas, and what did he give us?

What has William Smith been called? What did he find?

Between whom is another division in society?

B.

What may be injected into the veins of a man who is suffering from anaemia?

What are the enlightened farmers ready to do?

What do two thirds of all the people who live on the earth today do?

What has been done to provide homes for the families?

Into how many classes can society be divided?

What did Brillouin do?

Where did Smith find the fossils?

Explain another division in society.

Sayfa 226

Alıştırmalar

b) WHICH - olan, olduğu, olmuş olduğu

Sayfa 227

173. Aşağıda verilen cümledeki 'which' ile başlayan sıfat cümleciklerini kerre içine alıp nitelediği isimden önce yerleştiriniz. Sonra cümleyi Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Honest trade unions which serve their members are important in modern society.

Israel is a country which has a highly-developed co-operative system.

Nations which are without machines want to obtain them as soon as possible.

Sometimes old societies which take on new ways lose the best of their own traditions.

A society which wishes to use machines must teach all its children to read and write.

In Israel there is a nation-wide network of trade unions which share power with the State.

The movements of the body which follow messages which have been carried to the brain are directed to meet practical demands of the body.

Haemoglobin is the protein which makes blood red and which transports oxygen from the lungs to the tissues.

Animals can only respond to events which they notice.

Birds, which are the descendants of earlier reptiles, have well-developed colour vision.

We do not know much about memory which is a store of past perceptions which influence future action.

A cell has a surface membrane which limits its boundaries. The nucleus contains the material which determines the type of cell.

Muscles are made of cells which contain fibres which can shorten and then lengthen again.

Motor nerves are the nerves which lead to the muscles.

Sensory nerves are the nerves which carry information to the spinal cord or brain.

The proportion of the earth's surface which can actually be settled by human beings is comparatively small.

The work which can be carried out by all the members of the committee is explained in this report.

One great change which took place in this century was the mass-production of cars.

Iron is often used in the form of alloys which are harder and stronger than the pure metal.

Madeira, which is considered part of Portugal, is an island in the Atlantic Ocean which is about 400 miles west of Morocco.

Sayfa 228

Food should be protected from flies which can contaminate it with the bacteria which cause food poisoning.

The great force which is exerted by atmospheric pressure was demonstrated by von Guericke.

Galileo built the first telescope which showed the moon ten times closer. Today there are telescopes which bring the moon 360 times closer.

174. Alıştırma

Aşağıda yazılan cümleleri tercüme ediniz:

In the beginning the earth was a ball of burning gases which slowly cooled.

Catalysts are substances which enable a chemical action to take place but which do not themselves play any active part in the reaction.

Organic substances which were deposited with mud and sand during many thousands of years were completely transformed.

The skin is naturally greased by an oil which is produced by certain glands which lie just below the surface.

Sayfa 229

The central nucleus of an atom consists mainly of single particles of two kinds which are called protons and neutrons.

Particles which rotate round the nucleus are called electrons.

The neutrons which all atoms except hydrogen contain do not affect the electrical balance of the atom.

Certain bacteria which live only on the roots of certain plants extract nitrogen from the air.

At last Pasteur produced a vaccine which was successful against rabies.

Rivers may bring down large quantities of mud which spreads over a wide area.

The Bank of England and the Stock Exchange which helped people to raise capital enabled new enterprises to be undertaken.

A number of railways which have recently been constructed have brought the hinterland within easy reach of the coast.

The cold which was so intense during March has delayed the development of the buds on the fruit trees.

Repeated ploughing which promotes oxidation has ruined large areas of good soil in tropical countries.

The underground movement of great masses of molten magma which are so important cannot be observed at the surface.

Sözlük

to affect: tesir etmek, etki etmek

balance: denge

bud: tomurcuk

burning: yanan

capital: sermaye, anapara

catalyst: katalizatör, katalizör

certain: muayyen, belirli

coast: sahil, kıyı

to cool: soğumak

completely: tamamen

to consist of: -den meydana gelmek, oluşmak

to construct: döşemek, inşa etmek, kurmak

to contain: ihtiva etmek, içermek

to delay: geciktirmek

to deposit: çökmek, birikmek

to enable: mümkün kılmak, imkan vermek

enterprise: ticari iş, girişim

to extract: çıkarıp almak, özünü çıkarmak

gland: bez, gudde

to grease: yağlamak

hinterland: denizden uzak kara, ard ülke

intense: şiddetli, yoğun

just: hemen, tam, sadece

mainly: başlıca, esasen

molten: erimiş

mud: çamur

naturally: tabii olarak, doğal olarak

nitrogen: azot

to observe: gözetlemek, gözlemlemek

oil: yağ

particle: parçacık

to play a part: rol oynamak

rabies: kuduz

railway: demiryolu

reach: ulaşma, menzil

c) WHERE (olan yer, olduğu yer)

Alıştırma

175. Aşağıda yazılan cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

It is interesting to consider Chinese communities where university teachers and graduates must also work in the rice fields.

In the traditional society of agriculture in Britain where the peasant owned his land, each man was his own master.

They wanted to form a community where the members would govern themselves.

Votes of 99 per cent are generally found in totalitarian countries where it is dangerous not to vote.

Here is the factory where these goods are manufactured.

This is the place where the goods are stored before delivery.

The danger of disease lies in the places where the water is stored.

Women go to the communal oven where they bake their bread.

The caves where primitive man lived were cold and uncomfortable.

Most plants grow in places where soil and air are available.

It is much healthier to live in a wide street where sunlight can reach every house.

In areas where pine trees are grown extensively the risk of fire is serious.

Parasites can enter the body through places where there are openings, such as the nose, the mouth, or a cut in the skin.

People who live in a region where the parasite of a particular disease is common, build up a natural resistance to it.

Sayfa 231

A person from an area where antibodies to a certain disease are strong may carry the disease to another area where the population has not developed antibodies against it.

Penicillin can be injected into the blood where it destroys the parasite without damaging the cells.

Good crops were grown on the land where the new methods of farming were used.

Children in Europe where the war had left its results were examined and vaccinated against T.B.

Sözlük

antibody: antikor

available: mevcut, elde edilir

delivery: teslim, teslimat

to destroy: yok etmek

extensively: geniş sahalarda, yaygın olarak

fire: yangın

to form: kurmak, oluşturmak

generally: umumiyetle, genellikle

to govern: idare etmek, yönetmek

graduate: üniversite mezunu

healthy: sağlam, sıhhatli

to inject: zerk etmek, enjekte etmek

to manufacture: imal etmek, üretmek

member: üye

particular: muayyen, belirli, özel

peasant: köylü

percent: yüzde

d) WHOM (olan, olduğu, olmuş olduğu)

Ekseriyetle bir edat (preposition) ile birlikte kullanılır (Sayfa 234'e de bakınız).

Örnek: By whom, to whom, for whom, in whom, with whom (vs.)

Bu edat, cümleçikteki fiile bağlıdır. Türkçeye çevirince çoğu zaman edatı tercüme etmek lazım olmuyor.

Örnek: The teacher from whom he learned the language -> Lisanı öğrendiği öğretmen.

Türkçede düşüklük olursa veya anlamı açık değilse, bir iki kelime ilave edilerek düzeltilebilir:

Örnek: Kendisinden lisanı öğrendiği öğretmen.

Alıştırma

176. Aşağıda yazılan cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The farmers whom we had advised concerning their food crops were ready to experiment with new methods.

The men on whom the king depended to form a government came from the upper classes.

The artists by whom these pictures were painted had studied in Italy.

The peasants by whom the heaviest taxes were paid lived in great poverty.

The president whom the newspaper reporters interviewed explained his policy to the press.

The buyers to whom the goods were delivered had to pay for transport.

Sözlük

to advise: öğüt vermek, tavsiyede bulunmak

crop: mahsul, ürün

to deliver: teslim etmek, dağıtmak

to depend: güvenmek, bel bağlamak

government: hükümet

to interview: görüşmek, mülakat yapmak

to paint a picture: resim yapmak

peasant: köylü

policy: tutum, politika

poverty: sefalet, yoksulluk

president: reis, başkan, cumhurbaşkanı

the press: basın

reporter: gazeteci, muhabir

tax: vergi

transport: nakliyat, taşıma

upper: üst, yüksek (sınıf)

Sayfa 233

Anlama soruları

A.

Which farmers were ready to experiment with new methods?

Which men came from the upper classes?

Which artists had studied in Italy?

Who lived in great poverty?

Which president explained his policy to the press?

Which buyers had to pay for transport?

B.

What were the farmers ready to do?

Where did the men on whom the king depended come from?

Where had these artists studied?

How did these peasants live?

What did the president do?

What had the buyers to do?

e) Edat ile başlayan sıfat cümleciği

Örnek: from whom, to whom, with which, in which, to whose (vs.)

İngilizcede bu edat aslında cümleçikteki fiile bağlıdır.

Örnek:

We cut WITH a knife -> The knife WITH which we cut bread

We pay FOR a book -> The book FOR which we paid

We speak TO a person -> The person TO whom we spoke

We talk OF an idea -> The idea OF which we talked

Türkçeye çevirirken çoğu zaman bu edat tercüme edilmez. Yukarıdaki örnekler, mesela şöyle tercüme edilir:

The knife with which we cut bread: Ekmeği kestiğimiz bıçak

The book for which we paid: Ödediğimiz kitap

The person to whom we spoke: Konuştuğumuz şahıs

The land over which he ruled: Hükümet sürdüğü memleket

Eğer Türkçede bir düşüklük olacaksa, uygun bir edat bulup koyabiliriz:

The friend with whom she works: Birlikte çalıştığı arkadaş

The forest through which we went: İçinden geçtiğimiz orman

The trees through which the river ran: Nehrin arasından aktığı ağaçlar

Alıştırmalar

177. Aşağıdaki sıfat cümlelerini, nitelediği isimden önce yerleştirerek Türkçeye çeviriniz:

the substance with which the experiment was carried out

the method by which the substance was analysed

Sayfa 234

the fertilized cell from which we are developed

the way in which the subject is taught

an idea for which men have lived and died

limits beyond which the whole system breaks down

a contract under which the terms were agreed

a policy with which we disagree

an opportunity for which we have all been waiting

a theory according to which the universe originated at a finite time

an individual about whom nothing is known

a child for whom the state accepts responsibility

someone by whom the information was collected

a person with whom it is impossible to cooperate

a company from whom money can be borrowed

to borrow: ödünç almak

to carry out: icra etmek, yapmak

to collect: toplamak

to cooperate: iş birliği yapmak

company: şirket

contract: akit, mukavele, sözleşme

to develop: gelişmek, geliştirmek

to disagree: aynı fikirde olmamak, uyuşmamak

finite: muayyen, katî, sonlu

fertilised: döllenmiş

individual: fert, şahıs, birey

universe: kâinat, evren

whole: bütün

178. Aşağıda yazılan cümleleri yukarıdaki açıklamaya göre Türkçeye çeviriniz:

The language in which the report was written is difficult to translate.

Physics deals with the forces by which the particles of matter move or hold together.

The battle in which the soldiers died was fought on marshy ground.

The bottle in which the poison was kept is broken.

The steel workers held a meeting at which they decided future policy.

In the great gold mines in which primary deposits are found, the gold-bearing rocks are crushed.

The earth was covered with clouds from which rain fell for centuries.

The population of Wales is today about two and a half million, of which 2 million live in the towns.

The protruding surfaces are masses of granite from which the sur-

Sayfa 235

rounding rocks have been removed.

10. The first law of thermodynamics does not give any guidance as to the conditions under which changes from one form to another may occur.

11. The level of water in a well changes with the seasons, but there is a level below which the water normally never falls.

12. Asia gave us not only our religious beliefs but also the fundamentals upon which our civilisation is based.

Sözlük

as to: hususunda, konusunda, dair

to be based: temel olmak, dayanmak

battle: savaş

bearing: taşıyan, sahip olan

belief: inanç

civilisation: uygarlık, medeniyet

to crush: ezmek, kırmak

to deal with: ele almak, ilgili olmak

to decide: karar vermek

deposit: tortu, yatak, birikinti

force: kuvvet, güç

fundamental: esas, temel

granite: granit

guidance: rehberlik, fikir, yol gösterme

to hold together: bir arada tutmak

level: seviye

marshy: bataklık, bataklıklı

mine: ocak, maden ocağı

to occur: vuku bulmak, meydana gelmek

particle: parçacık

poison: zehir

policy: tutum, politika

primary: primer, ilk, birincil

protruding: çıkık, dışa fırlamış

to translate: tercüme etmek, çevirmek

Wales: Galler

well: kuyu

Anlama soruları

With which forces does physics deal?

Which bottle is broken?

f) - WHOSE ile başlayan sıfat cümleciği

Bu işaret kelimesi, İngilizcede iki isim arasında bulunur ve ikinci (yani takip eden) ismin, ilk isme ait bir varlık olduğunu ifade eder.

Örnek:

the girl whose arm (yani: kol, kıza aittir)

the man whose photograph (yani: fotoğraf, adama aittir)

Metnin devamı olan Sayfa 236 için yeni bir sayfa özetine veya incelemesine geçmemi ister misiniz?

Yüklediğiniz döküman, İngilizce dil bilgisi yapılarını (özellikle sıfat, isim ve zarf cümleliklerini) bilimsel, hukuki ve ekonomik metinler üzerinden açıklayan, egzersizler, kelime sözlükleri ve Anlama soruları

barındıran akademik bir kaynağa aittir.

Orijinal kaynak metinde yer alan tüm sayfalar (Metindeki sayfa numaralarıyla: Sayfa 237 - Sayfa 276), OCR kaynaklı harf ve kelime hatalarından (örneğin; filosofa -> filozofa, bankcrupt -> bankrupt, gahıs -> şahıs, nuleic -> nucleic, soild -> solid, univerdal -> universal gibi) tamamen arındırılarak, tek bir satır, sözlük kelimesi veya anlama sorusu atlanmaksızın sayfa sayfa aşağıda düzenlenmiştir:

--- SAYFA 237 ---

the boy whose family

the philosopher whose ideas

the atom whose electrons

(yani: aile, çocuğa aittir)

(yani: fikirler filozofa aittir)

(yani: elektronlar atoma aittir)

Bundan anlaşılır ki Türkçeye çevirirken bu münasebeti belli ettirmek doğru olur.

Örnek: * The girl whose arm is broken  Kolu kırılmış olan kız

The man whose photograph I saw  Fotoğrafını gördüğüm adam

The boy whose family was killed  Ailesi öldürülmüş olan çocuk

The atom whose electrons rotate  Elektronları devreden atom

Alıştırmalar

180. Yukarıdaki açıklama ve örneklere göre aşağıda yazılan cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

He found himself in a city whose inhabitants spoke a different language.

The simplest atom is that of hydrogen whose nucleus is a single proton with one electron.

Lithium, whose nucleus consists of three protons and three neutrons is a metal of the alkali group.

Particles which rotate round the nucleus are called electrons whose electrical charge is negative.

Poplar trees whose timber is in great demand for industry are grown in Europe on a large scale.

Among international organisations, the World Health Organisation whose task is to help in the fight against disease and starvation, depends upon help and cooperation from many different nations.

A teacher is a kind of doctor whose purpose it is to cure his patients of childishness and immaturity.

Extensive reading is possible for people whose English is good enough for them to use this book.

Scattered light should contain a component whose frequency is the sum of its original frequency, and that of the fluctuation in the dielectric constant.

Plants on whose roots colonies of bacteria were found to be growing were first thought to be suffering from some kind of disease.

Anlama Soruları

What kind of component should scattered light contain?

Which plants were first thought to be suffering from some kind of disease?

g) İşaret Kelimesi Olmayan Sıfat Cümlecikleri

Bazı sıfat cümleciklerinde, hiçbir işaret kelimesi (relative pronoun) yoktur. Bunlar ancak fiilleri bulunarak ana cümleden ayrılabilir.

Örnek: The things we eat should be clean. İki fiil yan yana düşüyor: (eat ve should be). Oradan anlaşılır ki sıfat cümleciği vardır. (we eat) = yediğimiz.

$$\text{Yediğimiz şeyler temiz olmalıdır.}$$

The people they met were foreigners. İki fiil yan yana düşüyor: (met ve were). Yani (they met) sıfat cümleciğidir.

$$\text{Tanıştıkları insanlar ecnebiydiler (yabancıydılar).}$$

Alıştırmalar

181. Aşağıdaki sıfat cümleciklerini nitelediği isimden önce yerleştirerek Türkçeye çeviriniz:

182. Yukarıdaki açıklama ve örneklere göre aşağıda verilen cümleleri tercüme ediniz:

Almost everything we eat, and everything other living things eat was once alive or part of something living.

The final general fact about life we need to remember is dealt with in the next chapter.

IV. İSİM CÜMLECİĞİ (NOUN CLAUSES)

İsim cümleciği bir ismin vazifesini yapar. Bir ismin yerini tutar.

Örnek: I did not know this. "This" kelimesini silip yerine bir cümlecik koyarsak isim cümleciği olur:

Ana Cümle

İsim Cümleciği

Türkçe Karşılığı

I did not know

where he lived.

Nerede oturduğunu bilmiyordum.

I did not know

what you said.

Söylediğinizi bilmiyordum.

I did not know

that you were ill.

Hasta olduğunuzu bilmiyordum.

I did not know

if you were coming.

Gelip gelmeyeceğinizi bilmiyordum.

--- SAYFA 241 ---

Ana Cümle

İsim Cümleciği

Türkçe Karşılığı

I did not know

whether you were coming.

Gelip gelmeyeceğinizi bilmiyordum.

Bu örneklerde mühim olan üç tür isim cümleciği gösterilmiştir. Bunlar aşağıda birer birer ele alınacaktır:

a) Soru kelimesi ile başlayan

b) 'that' ile başlayan

c) 'if' veya 'whether' ile başlayan

Her bir tür için alıştırmalar aşağıda verilmiştir.

a) Soru Kelimesi ile Başlayan İsim Cümleciği

Soru kelimelerinin en mühimleri şunlar olup Türkçe karşılıkları verilmiştir:

Soru Kelimesi

Türkçe Karşılığı

what

ne

why

niçin, neden

how

nasıl

how much

ne kadar

how many

kaç, kaç tane

how long

ne kadar zaman, ne kadar süre

where

nerede, nereye

when

ne zaman

who

kim

whom

kimi, kime

whose

kimin

which

hangi

which (one)

hangisi

NOT: Cümleyi tercüme ederken 'what'dan başka her birinin Türkçe karşılığını kullanmak doğru olur.

I. ('what' ile başlayan): Çoğu zaman 'what' kelimesi tek başına "ne" olarak tercüme edilmez, "-diği şey" yapısına dönüşür.

183. Alıştırma

Aşağıda yazılan cümlelerin isim cümleciğini parantez (veya daire) içine alıp tercüme ettikten sonra ana cümleye bağlayarak Türkçeye çeviriniz:

Advertisements often persuade people to buy what they do not want.

The effects of events continue to influence what is being done.

In running an animal does not simply repeat the same movements. What he does depends upon what he did last and upon what he perceives of the ground surface.

A person remembers what he wants to remember, that is, what interests him.

An individual remembers what he has to remember, that is, what is forced upon him by external and internal stresses.

What is alleged to be remembered sometimes differs in various ways from what actually happened.

Experiment can discover what sort of differences are most likely to occur and under what conditions the differences are likely to occur.

What is perceived and what is remembered are largely shaped by the names used at the time.

The change from what is essentially a Stone Age community to a modern university can be in twenty years.

--- SAYFA 242 ---

What animals perceive differs from what human beings perceive.

Different animals respond differently to what they perceive.

Much of what the early Greek philosophers taught was based on certain rigid rules.

The science of phenology studies what changes occur in the plant during its lifetime.

What happens when we eat starch is explained in the next chapter.

--- SAYFA 243 ---

(Diğer soru kelimeleri ile başlayanlar): Bu soru kelimeleri Türkçe karşılıklarıyla tercüme edilir.

184. Alıştırma

Aşağıda yazılan cümlelerin isim cümleciğini parantez içine alıp tercüme ettikten sonra ana cümleye bağlayınız:

In recent years our understanding of how animals and plants work has advanced in two directions.

First we know more about how the individual functions.

We have also learnt how the population as a whole functions and how it fits in with other animals and plants in its environment.

If we know enough about how the mosquitoes live and breed we can interfere with their breeding sites.

Mental ability cannot be judged from how much a person knows. The important thing to judge is how he uses the information.

The world is trying to discover how the planning of a modern industrial society can be combined with individual freedom.

The owner (either individuals or public corporations) can decide how much a worker is paid and how many hours he should work.

The city-states of medieval Europe discussed how a man ought to behave towards others.

It is not known precisely how or when in evolution perception first helped the direct bodily control of behaviour.

We do not know who invented the wheel, or how many times it was invented.

Despite its comparatively simple anatomy, each virus particle knows how it can reproduce itself.

The answer to why some kinds of animals behave in one way and some in another is a physiological answer.

Biologists knew a great deal about how this caterpillar lived in its native environment.

Copernicus showed how the observation of the motions of heavenly bodies could be explained if the earth and planets were supposed to move around the sun.

Newton suggested how an infinite primeval gas which filled space, would condense into stars.

In the Middle Ages, final victory in a war might depend on which army caught typhus first.

One of the most difficult questions of our time is how Africa can emerge with what is good in both the new and the old worlds.

--- SAYFA 244 ---

b) 'that' ile Başlayan İsim Cümleciği

NOT: Bu cins isim cümleciğini iki şekilde tercüme etmek mümkündür:

i) I did not know that he was ill.  Onun hasta olduğunu bilmiyordum.

ii) I did not know that he was ill.  Bilmiyordum ki hasta idi.

--- SAYFA 245 ---

Mümkün olduğu kadar ilk şekil tercih edilir ise de, cümle çok uzun olduğunda ikinci şekilde de tercüme edilebilir.

185. Alıştırma

Aşağıda verilen cümleleri yukarıda gösterildiği gibi tercüme ediniz:

Leeuwenhoek found that all water contained living creatures.

With a large number of experiments Pasteur proved that he was right.

Many scientists believe that there is a mass of metallic iron at the centre of the earth.

We find that most things contain iron or its alloys.

We hope that deadly nuclear weapons will not be used to destroy civilisation.

Copernicus maintained that the sun was the centre of the universe, and that all heavenly bodies revolved around it.

As a result of his calculations, Halley was able to state that a comet would appear in the year 1758.

There is no geological evidence to show that the continent existed.

Ptolemy believed that the earth was the centre of the universe, but he knew that it was a sphere.

The law of the conservation of matter states that matter and energy cannot be destroyed.

The final result is that the carbon is combined with oxygen to form carbon dioxide.

Many people believed that the earth was flat and that it was the centre of the universe.

In the past, scientists thought that all combustible materials contained a substance called phlogiston.

They believed that phlogiston must have a negative weight. This means that it must weigh less than nothing.

An English naturalist showed that plants had the power to purify the air by removing the carbon dioxide from it.

The law provides that every man should have a fair trial, and that no-one may be detained without a trial.

The law also provides that legislation should not be arbitrary and that the powers of the police should be limited.

Nearly everyone agrees that some amount of central government is necessary.

A hundred years ago Prout suggested that all atoms might be structures built of hydrogen atoms.

Lenard showed that electrons could pass through atoms and that the greatest part of the atom must be empty space.

Democracy means that responsibility is decentralised and shared by individuals.

--- SAYFA 246 ---

Educationists agree that the most satisfactory size for a class is between 8 and 15.

Common sense demands that the principles of non-violence should be applied not after, but before conflict has broken out.

The administrator and the anthropologist have discovered by experience that non-violence is the best and most practical policy.

Sözlük

Anlama Soruları

What do many scientists believe?

What is there no geological evidence to show?

What does the law of conservation of matter state?

What is the final result?

What did many people believe?

What did scientists think in the past?

--- SAYFA 247 ---

What did they believe? What does this mean?

What did an English naturalist show?

What does the law provide?

What does the law also provide? (two things)

What does nearly everyone agree?

What did Prout suggest 100 years ago?

What did Lenard show? (two things)

What does democracy mean?

What do educationists agree?

What does common sense demand?

What have the administrator and the anthropologist discovered by experience?

c) 'if' veya 'whether' ile Başlayan İsim Cümleciği

Bu yapılar Türkçeye "-ip olmadığı", "-ip olmayacağı" şeklinde çevrilir.

Alıştırmalar

186. a) Aşağıda yazılan cümleleri tercüme ederken, isim cümleciğindeki fiilin zamanına göre 'olup olmadığı' veya 'olup olmayacağı' gibi uygun bir karşılık kullanılmalıdır.

Primitive people knew if wild plants were poisonous or not.

Scientists wanted to find out if the ability of the virus to reproduce itself was in the nucleic acid or in the protein or in both.

Scientists still do not know if viruses should be regarded as living organisms or not.

For many centuries people have wondered if the other side of the moon resembles the side facing us.

Halley calculated the orbits of twenty-four comets to see if any of them passed along its previous path.

We must discover if we understand fully the meaning of the word 'nation'.

Scientists in the past have often wondered if it would be possible to see the other side of the moon.

Sözlük

İngilizce

Türkçe

to calculate

hesap etmek

comet

kuyruklu yıldız

facing

dönük, bakan

meaning

anlam, mana

orbit

yörünge

path

yol

poisonous

zehirli

previous

daha önce, önceki

primitive

ilkel

to regard

saymak, addetmek

to reproduce

çoğaltmak, üremek

to resemble

benzemek

wild

yabani

186. b) Şimdi yukarıdaki cümleler aşağıda tekrar yazılmıştır. Bu sefer 'if' yerine 'whether' yazılmıştır. Manada hiçbir fark yoktur. Cümleleri sözlüğe bakmadan Türkçeye çeviriniz:

--- SAYFA 248 ---

Primitive people knew whether wild plants were poisonous or not.

Scientists wanted to find out whether the ability of the virus to reproduce itself was in the nucleic acid or in the protein or in both.

Scientists still do not know whether viruses should be regarded as living organisms or not.

For many centuries people have wondered whether the other side of the moon resembles the side facing us.

Halley calculated the orbits of twenty-four comets to see whether any of them passed along its previous path.

We must discover whether we understand fully the meaning of the word 'nation'.

Scientists in the past have often wondered whether it would be possible to see the other side of the moon.

Anlama Soruları

What did primitive people know?

What did scientists want to find out?

What do scientists still not know?

What have people wondered for many centuries?

Why did Halley calculate the orbits of 24 comets?

What must we discover?

What have scientists often wondered in the past?

d) THE FACT THAT Strüktürü

Açıklama: Bu tabirin tercümesi ekseriyetle şöyle yapılır: 'that' kelimesinden sonra gelen fiil bulunup isim şekline çevrilir:

Örnek:

the fact that it grows  onun büyümesi

the fact that it is impossible  onun mümkün olmaması

the fact that it was discovered  onun keşfedilmesi

the fact that everyone was tired  herkesin yorgun olması

the fact that soil was good  toprağın iyi olması

the fact that he could not come  onun gelememesi

Alıştırmalar

187. Yukarıdaki örneklere ve açıklamaya göre aşağıda yazılan tabirleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

188. Aşağıda verilmiş olan cümleler 'the fact that' strüktürü kullanmaktadır. Bu strüktürü ayrı olarak tercüme ettikten sonra bütün cümleyi Türkçeye çeviriniz:

All evidence points clearly to the fact that there is a maximum size for working groups.

This country owed most of its prosperity to the fact that it was an island.

Oak should be planted only in deep fertile brown soils, owing to the fact that it does not grow well in shallow light soils.

Improvements could not be made until late in the nineteenth century owing to the fact that the new methods depended upon cheap electricity.

--- SAYFA 250 ---

Nitrogen must be added to the soil owing to the fact that plants do not grow well without it.

The fact that votes from those districts were not valid under the old law created many difficulties at election time.

The fact that many of the laws were not enforced made it impossible to maintain security and order.

The plants died during the cold weather owing to the fact that their roots were exposed.

Devastation of the area was assisted by the fact that the soil was eroded.

The fact that the land lies in the temperate zone makes it possible to grow a great variety of crops.

The fact that the rainfall is highest in spring when mountain snow is melting greatly increases the danger of floods on the plains.

Danger of infection in a deep wound is increased by the fact that certain micro-organisms can live without oxygen.

New insecticides are needed, because of the fact that many types of insect have developed a resistance to DDT.

The fact that a healthy man has a higher resistance to disease must never be forgotten.

Carbon-dating depends on the fact that radio-active carbon disintegrates at a constant rate.

We should be alarmed by the fact that the majority of civilised people cannot live happily without the stimulus of the mass-media: cinema, TV and radio.

to create

yaratmak, oluşturmak

to depend on

Anlama Soruları

To what fact does all evidence point clearly?

To what fact did this country owe most of its prosperity?

Why should oak be planted only in deep fertile brown soils?

Why could improvements not be made until late in the 19th century?

Why must nitrogen be added to the soil?

What fact created many difficulties at election time?

What fact made it impossible to maintain security and order?

What fact greatly increases the danger of floods on the plains?

V. It + to be + sıfat / past part. + that İle Başlayan İsim Cümleciği

Örnek: It is clear that the machine has been used.

Açıklama: Makinenin kullanılmış olduğu bellidir.

It must be remembered that he is very young.

$$\text{Çok genç olduğu hatırlanmalıdır.}$$

It is thought that he is guilty.

$$\text{Suçlu olduğu zannediliyor.}$$

Cümlenin tercüme edilmesinde güçlüğe uğranılırsa, 'that'den sonra gelen parçayı (yani, isim cümleciğini) ayrı olarak, normal bir ana cümle gibi tercüme ediniz.

Örnek: It must be remembered that Britain had a well-developed river-system before the Great Ice Age.

'that'den sonraki cümleciği, ayrı bir ana cümle gibi:

Britain had a well-developed river-system before the Great Ice Age.

$$\text{Büyük Buz Çağından önce, Britanya'nın iyi gelişmiş bir nehir sistemi vardı.}$$

Sonra, 'It must be remembered'  Hatırlanmalıdır.

Birleştirilir:

$$\text{Büyük Buz Çağından önce Britanya'nın iyi gelişmiş bir nehir sistemi bulunduğu hatırlanmalıdır.}$$

veya

$$\text{Hatırlanmalıdır ki, Büyük Buz Çağından önce Britanya'nın iyi gelişmiş bir nehir sistemi vardı.}$$

--- SAYFA 252 ---

Alıştırma

189. Yukarıdaki örneklere göre aşağıda yazılan cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

It was evident that the forests in the areas would not survive for long.

It is believed that nothing can travel faster than electro-magnetic waves.

It has been explained that the body can also extract energy from sugars.

It became clear that goats were one of the main causes of forest devastation.

It was observed that many tree-seeds could germinate on the surface of the soil.

It is known that there is a mass of metallic iron at the centre of the earth.

It has been calculated that the electron rotates round the nucleus seven million milliard times per second.

It might be thought that birds flying from the northern to the southern hemisphere every year always follow the same route, but this is not so.

It used to be believed that the earth was the centre of the universe.

It is supposed that the first plants to appear on earth lived in the sea.

It has been shown that green plants have the power to purify the air by removing the carbon dioxide from it.

It is often found that the parasite and the host live together in close relationship.

It is believed that true freedom is impossible without discipline.

It is hoped that deadly nuclear weapons will not be used to destroy civilisation.

It used to be thought that all combustible material contained a substance called phlogiston.

It is clearly stated that no one may be detained without a trial.

It is accepted that changes are not made in the Factory Acts without consulting the Trade Unions.

It is accepted that changes are not made in the Health Service without consulting the British Medical Association.

It is found by experiment that group activities become difficult with more than 20 individuals.

It has never been proved scientifically that the continent of Atlantis has ever existed.

--- SAYFA 253 ---

Alıştırma

190. Yukarıdaki örneklere göre aşağıda yazılan cümleleri Türkçeye çeviriniz:

It must be remembered that the British Isles had a well-developed river system before the Great Ice Age.

It was formerly assumed that the submerged forests round the shores of Britain were all of the same age.

It will be clear that the Welsh Massif was built up by successive mountain-building movements.

It has long been known that the solid rocks in the earth's crust contain the remains of animals and plants.

--- SAYFA 254 ---

It was found that, when a species died out, its fossils did not reappear in later rocks.

It is clear that there is a definite cycle of igneous activity associated with the cycle of earth movements.

It is known that there is a close relationship between the character of a river and the phase of the erosion cycle.

It is very important that the humus content of the soil is maintained.

It has been emphasised that the formation of soil from the parent material is mainly the work of circulating waters.

It is evident that the soils of Britain vary very greatly in natural fertility.

It has been suggested that the composition of the earth's atmosphere may have been different from today.

It has been suggested that a larger proportion of carbon dioxide in the earth's atmosphere may have encouraged growth of vegetation in the Coal Measure times.
